Talks by Weng Wenhao: Recent Developments in Sino-Japanese Diplomacy and Local Administration; University Student Training Program Scheduled to Start in September 20

(Nanjing) Regarding recent Sino-Japanese diplomacy, the central government's reforms to local administration, and the progress of the university student training program, a reporter from the Central News Agency visited Weng Wenhao on the 24th to inquire about his views. According to his account, with regard to recent issues between China and Japan, Japanese Ambassador Kawagoe repeatedly discussed and exchanged views with Foreign Minister Zhang, expressing his opinions frankly and sincerely regarding the general adjustment of diplomatic relations, in addition to explaining the solutions considered by the Chinese government. Although no concrete solutions have been agreed upon, it is believed that both China and Japan will adopt an impartial attitude to clarify the general issues. The Executive Yuan has been very proactive this year in researching and reforming local administration, aiming to determine, enrich, and improve the organization of counties, the powers of administrative commissioners, and local security within a short period. The Chairman's headquarters has introduced many innovations for the reform of local systems, such as the joint office of the provincial government, the establishment of supervisory commissioners, the restructuring of county governments by replacing bureaus with sections, and the establishment of public offices, which have proven effective in implementation. However, because the scope is limited to bandit suppression areas and there are still many issues that need to be improved, the Executive Yuan convened a conference of commissioners in May to discuss the actual situation of local administration, aiming to promote benefits and eliminate drawbacks. After the conference, the Premier immediately assigned two counselors, Zhang and Wu, to visit Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi to inspect the situation, with very satisfactory results. Politics in various regions have shifted from passive to active, but there are still many areas that need improvement. The Executive Yuan has also assigned personnel to study the joint office of the provincial government, the organization of administrative commissioners, the establishment of sub-regional offices, the preservation of armor and grain, and security, in order to find effective reform methods. Once compiled, these methods will be implemented. Subsequently, local administrative inspectors will be dispatched to various regions to inspect local political institutions and the national economy. Weng mentioned that the enrollment of students for the training program for graduates of specialized schools and universities has been completed, and the situation is very good. The qualification review is based on a common and appropriate percentage of the number of graduates from each school in the most recent three years, calculating the number of places each school can enroll. If the number of recommended students exceeds the quota, those with lower academic performance will be eliminated. This allows for an assessment of the quality of each school's management. Overall, the review results show that the percentage of students in science and engineering is the lowest, while the liberal arts are more numerous, indicating a lack of practical talent in China. All preparations for the training program have been completed, and it is scheduled to begin in September. After the training, graduates will be assigned for internships and employment. The location of assignment has not yet been determined. (Central News Agency dispatch, 24th)

China Obtains Council Seat in League of Nations; Committee of League of Nations Passes Resolution; Gu Weijun Speaks on China's Position; Executive Council to Increase to Fifteen Members 32

(Geneva) The First Committee of the League of Nations, namely the Legal and Regulatory Committee, held a public meeting this morning, chaired by the Dutch representative Limburg, to discuss the organization of the Executive Council.

Regarding this matter, Argentina, Australia, Belgium, the United Kingdom, Canada, Spain, France, Iran, Italy, Peru, Poland, Sweden, the Soviet Union, and China had previously formed a committee on the allocation of Executive Council seats to conduct research. In April of this year, they resolved to make a recommendation to the General Assembly that the organization of the Executive Council should be changed. The non-permanent council seat previously obtained by Portugal in 1933 should also be maintained after its term expires this year. At the same time, an additional seat should be added for China, increasing the number of Executive Council members from fourteen to fifteen.

At today's meeting of the Legal and Regulatory Committee, the Norwegian representative expressed dissatisfaction with the current organization of the Executive Council, stating that the countries of South America occupied three seats on the Executive Council (namely Ecuador, Chile, and Argentina), which was too many, and that the number of Executive Council members was constantly increasing, and that in a few years, their number would be equal to that of the League of Nations General Assembly. In addition, Chile, Argentina, and Venezuela supported the proposal to change the organization of the Executive Council. As for the various proposals to amend the League Covenant, the committee decided to postpone further discussion until the next General Assembly. (24th Havas)

(Geneva) The Chinese representative, Dr. Gu Weijun, the country's ambassador to France, gave a speech on the country's request for a council seat, stating that since 1934, there had been no representative of an Asian country on the Executive Council, but the Executive Council should be all-encompassing, and events occurring in Asia could affect the entire world, and the Executive Council would benefit from directly obtaining information. "China has a vast territory and abundant resources," and its population is the largest in the world. Its cooperation with the League of Nations has been extremely close from the beginning, and it is very appropriate to represent Asia.

The representatives of Chile, Caballer, Iran, Atle, Siam, Vatravandi, Turkey, Sadok, and Iraq, Nuri, all supported China's request. The First Committee then passed a resolution proposing to the League of Nations General Assembly that the number of non-permanent Executive Council members be increased from nine to eleven, one of which would be given to China, and one would be retained by Portugal. (24th Havas Dispatch)

League of Nations General Assembly Passes Resolution Allowing Abyssinia to Continue Attendance; Case Submitted to World Court Dismissed 33

(Geneva) The Credentials Committee of the League of Nations decided today that the Abyssinian delegation may continue to attend and enjoy the rights of a member state. It is generally believed that Italy's withdrawal from the League of Nations is likely unavoidable.

The Credentials Committee convened several meetings today. In addition to the above decision, it also decided that the credentials of the Abyssinian delegation were legitimate and should not be requested for adjudication by the International Court of Justice in The Hague, because since the Abyssinian representatives had been permitted to attend the General Assembly temporarily, requesting a ruling from the Hague Court would only further complicate the issue. The report of the Credentials Committee allowing the Abyssinian representatives to attend the League of Nations General Assembly was subsequently passed by the General Assembly with a majority of 39 votes to 4. Six countries abstained from the vote. When the Greek representative Politis handed the Credentials Committee report to the Abyssinian representative Taezaz, Taezaz expressed his gratitude upon receiving it. Subsequently, the Hungarian representative suddenly rose and questioned Abyssinia's right to attend, shocking the entire assembly. Representatives from Albania and Australia also supported Hungary's opinion.

The Swiss representative Motta said he would not participate in the vote because the issue of the legitimacy of the Abyssinian delegation's credentials still existed and its political implications were significant.

The votes in favor were from the United Kingdom, France, the Little Entente, and the Balkan Alliance countries, as well as the British Dominions. The votes against were from Hungary, Austria, Albania, and Ecuador. The countries that abstained were Bulgaria, Chile, Siam, Switzerland, Portugal, and Venezuela.

The Credentials Committee's action is only valid for the current session. The Committee's decision to oppose appealing to the Hague International Court of Justice is because the Hague International Court of Justice cannot make any ruling before the League of Nations General Assembly closes. (23rd Reuters Dispatch)

(Geneva) At the meeting, the reporter of the Credentials Committee, the Greek representative Politis, first read the report of the committee. The Abyssinian youth representative, Taezaz, immediately stood up and expressed his thanks to the Credentials Committee in a few words. The Hungarian representative, General Thomazos, then proposed that the General Assembly vote on the matter by roll call. The representatives of Austria and Albania seconded the proposal. The Swiss representative, Mutta, expressed the opinion that "whether Abyssinia can attend the General Assembly is not merely a procedural issue. The Credentials Committee's decision not to submit this issue to the Hague Permanent Court of International Justice is indeed wise. However, the question of whether the Abyssinian representatives' qualifications are valid still exists and will inevitably have extremely important political consequences. Therefore, Switzerland intends to abstain from voting."

The Chairman of the Credentials Committee, the Peruvian representative Tudela, immediately stood up to reply, saying that the issue of the Abyssinian representatives' qualifications, as far as the present is concerned, is purely a procedural issue, and that what the Credentials Committee can deal with is also limited to procedural issues. At that point, the Chairman of the General Assembly, the Argentinian Foreign Minister Lamas, used a roll call method to put the matter to a vote. It was estimated that a total of 49 member states of the League of Nations attended today's General Assembly. According to Article 5 of the League of Nations Covenant, matters concerning the procedures of the General Assembly are valid if passed by a majority. Therefore, the Abyssinian delegation obtained the right to attend the current General Assembly. It was already 8:15 PM, and the General Assembly was adjourned until 10:00 AM the next day. (23rd Havas Dispatch)

(Geneva) The Credentials Committee of the League of Nations General Assembly completed the review of the Abyssinian representatives' qualifications at 5:50 PM. The committee's review report was immediately issued. The report advocated allowing the Abyssinian representatives to attend the current General Assembly, but it clearly stated that this decision did not affect Abyssinia's legal status. As for the matter of seeking advice from the Hague Permanent Court of International Justice, the committee believed that there were practical inconveniences in fact, because, on the one hand, the International Court of Justice could not issue an advisory opinion until several weeks later, and, on the other hand, the issue of whether to allow Abyssinian representatives to appear in court to defend themselves would still arise when the International Court of Justice opened the court. However, the report did not mention what international repercussions this decision would have. When the report was issued, a large crowd gathered outside the hotel where the Abyssinian Emperor was staying, and the public gallery was also extremely crowded when the League of Nations General Assembly voted on the report. (23rd Havas Dispatch)

The current plan of the right-wing army is as follows: (1) Attack Toledo, cut off the communication of the left-wing army, and isolate the army surrounding the Alcázar fortress. (2) Defeat the army surrounding the Alcázar to rescue the right-wing cadets who have been trapped for six weeks. (3) Advance northeast, cutting off traffic from Madrid to Valencia. (4) Attack Madrid simultaneously from the northwest, northeast, and south. At the same time, the left-wing army also announced the following plan: (1) Occupy the Alcázar. (2) If it cannot be occupied, the army surrounding the fortress will try to retreat. (3) Use the army attacking the Alcázar to attack the rebel army advancing towards Madrid and merge with the main force of the government army. (4) Form a mobile wall between the rebel army and the capital. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Fortress Recaptured, Rebel Army Exhausted and Surrendered 40

Madrid – The siege of the historically famous Moorish fortress of Alcázar in Toledo ended today after a long period. Government troops have occupied the remaining fortresses. The fortress has been under siege for nine weeks. Although the rebel army was in a desperate situation, they fought to the death and used a small force to resist the masses. They were able to make government troops gain every inch of land only at a great cost. At dawn today, a stormtrooper of 400 government troops began to attack. The remaining rebel army in the fortress still occupied the dining room and kitchen as their final stand. Due to the disparity in numbers, they were finally exhausted and surrendered. Therefore, the fortress changed hands and fell into the hands of government troops. Spanish Prime Minister Caballero has set off for Toledo to reward the government troops who attacked the fortress. During the nine weeks that the fortress was under siege, for several weeks, the garrison only had one meal a day, consisting of a piece of horse meat and a small amount of bread. Among them, officer cadets and aristocratic children shared the hardships with the soldiers. The situation inside the fortress was very terrifying. Rotten corpses were everywhere. (Reuters, 23rd)

Madrid – According to a communique released by the government, government troops in Toledo completely occupied the Alcázar fortress this morning. Prime Minister Caballero has rushed to the city of Toledo to congratulate the government troops. Another communique said that government troops continued to attack the rebel vanguard in the city of Oviedo. Many rebel deserters surrendered. Government troops on the Estremadura front attacked the rebel army in the area of ​​Cuéllar, killing 400 people. Government troops on the Somosierra front have consolidated their original positions. There were small contacts on the Talavera front, but they were not of major strategic importance. (Havas, 23rd)

(Paris) According to news from Toledo, some rebels, carrying machine guns, were still in the Alcázar fortress, resisting government troops. However, after government troops occupied the kitchen, the rebel army had no place to seek food. It is heard that government troops will launch a new attack immediately. (Reuters, 24th)

Toledo – As of 7:00 AM this morning, the garrison of the Alcázar fortress was still stubbornly resisting and had not retreated. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Revolutionary Theory: Talk by Northern Route Commander 41

He said, "The Spanish nation is organized by various disparate factors. If we want to unite, we must have considerable authority. According to this, only the army can rule everything. The reason why the organization of the National Army government is based on various generals is because of this." Then he spoke about the organization of the military government, saying, "The military government is composed of a meeting of commanders from various routes, such as General Franco, commander-in-chief of the Southern Route, General Davila, a member of the military government, General Fonder, General Yagüe, commander of the troops stationed in the Moroccan territory, General Deriano, commander of the Andalusian division, and myself (General Mola referring to himself) all participate, and the military government chairman, General Cabanellas, presides over it. As for other administrative matters, there are several directors in charge, who are responsible for (1) commerce, (2) public works, (3) finance, (4) justice, and (5) propaganda. Among them, the director of justice is responsible for selecting judges and restoring civil courts. Criminal cases are still handled by military courts. As for propaganda matters, they are handled by Mr. Puijol, a former Madrid congressman who was a journalist, and he also publishes the "Gazette of the National Military Government". This organization will also be used as a blueprint when a formal government is established in the future." (Havas, 24th)

French Capital Continues to Flee, Cabinet Position Perilous, Gold Export Ban, Franc Devaluation, Rumors Rampant in London and Paris 43

(London) Rumors that the French cabinet will change soon, and news that Mr. Caillaux Renaud, who advocates lowering the value of the currency, suddenly returned to Paris from New York, caused the price of gold coins converted into pounds to continue to weaken this morning. The spot franc price fell to 77.00, and was maintained by the British Funds, and then returned to 76.98. The forward franc price fell even more, which reflects the weakness of the franc's position. Some believe that the reason for this is that the Dutch currency is based on the franc. The Dutch bank is afraid that the franc will collapse, so it sells a large number of forward francs and buys long-term US dollars. The forward US dollar has recently increased in premium converted into pounds, which is probably the reason for this. Although the Bank of France has lost as much as 4.5 million pounds of gold in the past few days, traders in the foreign exchange market are still skeptical about the rumors that France will implement a gold export ban, but it is generally recognized that this move will be realized sooner or later. (Reuters, 23rd)

Prelude to North China's Economic Exploitation: Japanese Plan to Dominate North China's Electric Power Industry; Two Companies, Toyo and Osaka, Establish Paper Mills 75

Tianjin Dispatch: The electric power project of the Xingzhong Company in North China aims to achieve domination based on the tactics of the Manchuria Electric Power Company. The Manchuria Electric Power Company's capital was increased to 50 million yuan. All public matters related to electricity, telephone, and streetcars in the four northeastern provinces, whether government-run or private, were bought up, and it has now achieved its goal of domination. Its ambition for the North China electricity industry is no less than its ambition in the Northeast, but it is afraid that its actions will easily attract attention, so it is using the Xingzhong Company as a front, while the Manchuria Electric Power Company is still responsible for the capital burden. In addition to the establishment of the Sino-Japanese joint venture Electric Power Joint Stock Company in Tianjin, it has recently also acquired the electric power industries in Qinhuangdao, Tangshan, Luankou (including Beidaihe and Liushouying), Nandasi, and Changli. For the electric power industries in Beiping and Zhangjiakou, power plants are planned to be built in the Qin, Tang, and Luan areas to control the electric power industries in the key towns along the Beining Railway line, develop light and heavy industries, and supply electricity to meet the needs of companies such as Zhongfang Textile, Shihe Rayon Factory, and Toyo Textile Company. In Beiping and Zhangjiakou, in addition to focusing on electric lights, attention is also being paid to suburban streetcars, and the construction of the Tangshan, Nankou, and Xiangshan streetcar lines is already in the planning stages. The Xingzhong Company plans to build a total of 350,000 kilowatts of power plants in the above-mentioned locations. The Tianjin plant will have 100,000 kilowatts. According to their investigation, the entire city of Tianjin currently has 80,000 kilowatts of electric power equipment, of which 15,000 kilowatts each are owned by the British and French concessions, and the remainder is owned by the Belgian tram and lighting company. In the future, after the company's new plant generates electricity, it will gradually acquire it to complete the entire electric power rights. If this cannot be realized temporarily, it will definitely supply 50,000 kilowatts of electricity to Special District 1, 3, the Japanese Concession, and the suburbs of Tianjin to surround the Belgian power plant, preventing it from developing and eventually forcing it to sell. It will also send electricity at low prices, allowing users to freely choose, as a tool for competition. Outside of Tianjin, 250,000 kilowatts of electricity will be distributed for construction in Ping, Tang, Qin, Zhang, and Luan. In the area east of Australia, the Luanhe and Shihe Rivers will be used for hydroelectric power, making construction easier. The Xingzhong Company also believes that for the economic development of North China, electric power is the pioneer of everything and domination must be achieved, so it has been actively engaged in this work recently. The Tianjin power plant has been expanded and reorganized in consultation with the Tianjin Municipal Government on the basis of the Xinji Electric Power Company in Special District 1, and renamed Tianjin Electric Power Co., Ltd. It was established on the 22nd, and is presided over by Hirayama, the Xingzhong resident director in Tianjin. There are more than 40 Chinese and Japanese employees. The site has not yet been surveyed, but construction will begin no later than late October and will be completed next October. The plant belongs to the Sino-Japanese joint venture Tianjin Electric Power Co., Ltd., and specializes in electric power. Suburban streetcars will be operated separately and will not begin construction until the power plant is built. The total amount of funds is 4 million yuan, borrowed from Japanese capital, which has been contacted by Hirayama. The Manchuria Electric Power Company will provide the capital. Although the contract has not been signed, there should be no major problems. The only difference is the repayment of principal and interest. Many local gentry and merchants in Tianjin are unwilling to have this public utility be seized by foreigners, so Zhao Ziyu and others have jointly petitioned the municipal government, requesting that they raise funds to manage it themselves, or operate it as a joint-stock company, attracting a small amount of Chinese capital, and not borrowing exclusively from Japanese loans. The municipal government specially convened Zhao and others for discussion on the morning of the 23rd and agreed to the investment proposal. However, it was said that it must be approved by the company's board of directors before a decision can be made. The Tianjin authorities have nothing to say, but the attitude of the Japanese side is still speculation.

Toyo Paper Manufacturing Co. plans to raise 20 million yuan to set up a paper mill because of the strong sales of western paper and newspapers in North China. The main factory is in Tokyo, and the first branch factory will be set up in Chentangzhuang or Dazhigu between Tanggu, Tianjin. It will use Huai from Hebei and Shandong and utilize the Haihe River's water conservancy to produce newsprint and general-purpose western paper. The planned production is 1,000 tons, which will be sold exclusively in North China. Uchida, the former director of the Taiwan Colonial Products Bureau, has been assigned to plan it. He came to Tianjin not long ago to conduct a preliminary investigation before starting factory construction. In addition, Osaka Joint Paper Manufacturing Co. also plans to raise 5 million yuan to purchase 3,000 acres of land in Dazhigu, Tianjin, to make paper from reeds growing locally. Construction work may be realized at the same time as Toyo Paper Manufacturing Co. (23rd)

An Important Page in the History of Transportation in the Southwest: Successful Trial Run of the Yunnan-Guizhou Highway; The Entire 600 Kilometers Can Be Reached in Four Days; Connection to Other Roads Allows Direct Access to Various Provinces in China 76

Kunming Correspondence: The Yunnan-Guizhou Highway, with a total length of 600 kilometers, has now been completed. Qiu Chuanmeng, secretary of the General Headquarters Highway Office, and others were dispatched to test the road, traveling in two buses. They departed from Guiyang on the 12th and arrived safely in Kunming at 7:00 PM on the 14th. The 600-kilometer journey used to take 20 days on foot, but now it can be reached safely in four days. Once the paving is completed and the entire road is unblocked, it can be reached in about two days. The route will be from Kunming to Panxian on one day, and from Panxian to Guiyang on the next. After opening to Guizhou, it will be possible to reach Hunan via the Hunan-Guizhou Railway, and then to various provinces across the country. This is truly an important page in the history of transportation in the southwest. Details are recorded as follows:

There are 18 stations between Kunming, Yunnan Province, and Guiyang, Guizhou Province. In the past, transportation was inconvenient, and it took about 20 days to reach on foot. After Chairman Long took charge of Yunnan, he prioritized transportation as a key policy for construction. He decided to devote all efforts to building highways throughout the province. The initial plan was to build four trunk roads and eight branch roads throughout the province. The road from Kunming to Panyi Shengguan is 229 kilometers long and is the main road in eastern Yunnan. Except for the 17-kilometer section from Kunming to Dabanciao, which was a dirt road built by the Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee during the relief efforts in 1926, the rest was surveyed and measured in January 1929. At the same time, earth road construction was started in sections. By 1931, the road was open to Yanglin, in 1932 to Qujing, and in 1933 to Panyi. The entire road was a difficult project. The dirt road was built by requisitioning laborers, and bridges and culverts above a certain size were built with provincial funds. Bridges below a certain size were built locally. The construction of bridges such as the Maguo River, Baishi River, and Yiqiao was particularly difficult. It is estimated that the projects built with provincial funds cost more than 2 million, and the earthwork and bridges and culverts built locally cannot be counted. The roadbed of the entire road is quite solid. After the paving is completed, it can pass trucks with a load of more than 15 tons. The gradient of the entire line is no greater than 8%, and the radius of curvature is no less than 48 feet, making driving quite safe. Even if a railway is built in the future, it can be used after some repairs. Currently, the paving work on the section from Kunming to Songming has been completed, and the section from Songming to Panyi is being carried out in sections and is expected to be completed by the end of the year.

The section of the Yunnan-Guizhou Highway within Guizhou Province, from Panyi to Panxian, is 60.85 kilometers long. Last year, it was ordered by Chairman Chiang to be built by Yunnan Province, with a central government subsidy of 150,000 yuan. Surveying began in June last year, and work was carried out actively, completing the project last month. A total of 200,000 yuan was spent. The section from Guiyang to Panxian includes the section from Guiyang to Huangcaishu, which is over 100 kilometers long and was completed during the reign of Zhou Xicheng in Guizhou, but it was not entirely perfect. The section from Huangguoshu to Panxian is 206 kilometers long. The General Headquarters Highway Office was ordered to build and reorganize the section from Guiyang to Huangguoshu last year. Surveying and construction began on September 11 last year, led by engineers Xu Mingjie and Zou Yuesheng in sections. It was completed on September 10 this year. The cost of each road is about 1 million yuan. The Banguan Slope special project is still in progress, but it does not hinder direct traffic.

After the completion of the Yunnan-Guizhou Highway, the General Headquarters Highway Office dispatched special commissioners to test the road. They departed from Guiyang on the 11th of this month. The Yunnan Provincial Government and the Road Bureau prepared a reception. The Road Bureau's Secretary Zhang and Chief Technician Li and others welcomed the travelers at Dabanciao at about 2:00 PM on the 14th, traveling in two cars. The vehicles from Guizhou arrived safely at 6:00 PM. The personnel from Guizhou who came to test the road included Qiu Chuanmeng, secretary of the General Headquarters Highway Office, engineering directors Xu Mingjie and Zou Yuesheng, General Headquarters supervisor Yin Haoyue, General Headquarters technician Ren Yongxu, Jian Gang, member of the Guizhou Pacification Commissioner's Office, and Xiao Weimin, a correspondent from the Central News Agency in Guizhou, a total of eleven people. All were hosted by the Road Bureau and stayed at Deyichun. After this road is opened to traffic, not only will transportation between Yunnan and Guizhou provinces become more convenient, but it will also be possible to establish links with the central government and the provinces along the Yangtze River. The Guizhou-Hunan Road can be used to reach Changsha in Hunan Province, as well as Jiangxi, Anhui, Hubei, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong, and other provinces. It will take only ten days to reach Hangzhou from Kunming. Its benefits to the transportation, culture, and national defense of the southwestern provinces are immeasurable. (22nd)

Niu Yongjian Requests Protection of Songjiang Fishermen's Livelihood 77

Regarding a dispute over maritime boundaries between Jiangsu and Zhejiang, fishermen from Jinshanzui, Songjiang County, were fishing at sea. Their fishing grounds have always been in the waters around Baishan. Recently, due to the jurisdictional issue over the Shengsi Islands in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, there has been a dispute over the demarcation of maritime boundaries. Both sides are arguing, as if it were a national border, causing the Baishan fishing grounds of the Jinshanzui fishermen to be designated by the fishermen of Baishawan, Pinghu County, Zhejiang Province, as belonging to Zhejiang territory, and people from other provinces are not allowed to fish. The fishing gear in the fishing grounds was wantonly destroyed, and force was used to refuse them. Niu Tiesheng, Vice President of the Examination Yuan, believed that this matter was related to the livelihood of the fishermen of Songjiang, and specially wrote to Shen, the Director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, requesting to take charge of protecting them. The original letter is transcribed below: "Mr. Baixian Jianjian, according to the letter from Mr. Zhang Mingguang of the Songjiang County Fishermen's Association, Jinshanzui in the southern part of Songjiang County faces the sea, and the coastline is more than thirty li long. The residents all make a living by fishing at sea. The fishing ground is on the Baishan sea surface southeast of Jinshanzui, commonly known as Hengdi. Every spring, stakes are driven and ropes are tied to set up nets for fishing, which stops at the Lesser Heat Festival. For generations, everyone has lived in peace. This spring, Pan Chunfu and Pan Fusheng from Baishawan, Pinghu County (more than 20 li west of Jinshanzui), coveted the Hengdi and led many people, carrying rifles, to break into the Hengdi fishing grounds of the Jinshanzui fishermen. They cut down 125 sets of fishing gear set up by Yang Qiusheng, Fan Ade, Lu Baogen, Wu Agui, and others. Mr. Shen was requested by telegram to ask Chairman Huang of Zhejiang Province to order Pinghu County to stop this, and the Songjiang County Fishermen's Association and the Songjiang County Government filed a petition to the Jiangsu Construction Department for relief. Unexpectedly, Pinghu County falsely claimed that the Baishan sea surface was under the jurisdiction of the county and sent a letter to the Songjiang County Magistrate ordering the Jinshanzui fishermen to automatically remove their fishing nets. As a result, Pan Chunfu and others became even more rampant and continued to carry out destruction in the Hengdi fishing grounds of the Jinshanzui fishermen. On the 17th of June, they cut down and looted 59 sets of fishing gear in the Hengdi of Yang Qiusheng, together with the fish, with losses totaling more than 4,000 yuan. The livelihood of the year has been completely cut off. Considering that the area in the sea is vast and the fish production is inexhaustible, the number of fishermen in Jinshanzui is small, and it should not hinder the livelihood of the fishermen in Zhejiang Province. Therefore, I respectfully ask you to transfer this matter to the Jiangsu Construction Department, send personnel for on-site inspection, and declare that the Baishan sea surface will always be the Jinshanzui fishing ground. On the one hand, please order Zhejiang Province to order Baishawan Pan Chunfu and others to compensate the Jinshanzui fishermen for their losses in full to relieve their difficulties. I have checked that the case of the dispute between the fishermen of Jinshanzui and Baishawan was previously requested by the Zhejiang Provincial Government to order the subordinates to stop it. Now, according to the letter, this case has been delayed and not resolved, and another huge loss was caused on June 17. Although there are boundary disputes between provinces and counties, the fishermen of the two provinces are all citizens of the country, and the fishermen of Jinshanzui seem to be small in number and should not be cut off from their livelihoods. At this time, when the country is in a serious situation, the fishermen on the coast should be trained and organized to know how to unite against foreign enemies. The actions of the fishermen of Baishawan are close to private fights, and this trend should not be allowed to grow. Mr. Shen is holding on to his pain, and I dare to turn around and ask you to select fair and appropriate personnel to work with Zhejiang Province for on-site inspection, and to discuss a fair solution so that the fishermen of the two provinces can benefit from it. The locality is fortunate. I hope you will understand this is fortunate, Niu Yongjian, Respectfully."

European Travel Correspondence 78

— The Conte Verde Arrives in Hong Kong (Continued)

— Xu Shu

Arrived in Hong Kong at eight o'clock in the morning on the 30th. People who have been to Hong Kong are eager to say goodbye, while those who have never been there naturally want to visit. After two days and two nights of sailing, they should see the land. After two days and two nights of foreign meals, they should switch to Japanese flavors, so almost everyone went ashore.

We mailed letters and bought some things, and then wanted to hire a car to tour all of Hong Kong. Our group had a total of six people. We hired a car at China Travel Service. The car that place managed to get was a private chauffeured car, and was stopped by a Chinese policeman. We all went to the police station of what the policeman called "our government." The policeman spoke very fiercely, but when he arrived at "our government," he was no longer powerful. The translator told us that private chauffeured cars were prohibited from doing business, to prevent drivers from earning money privately. Since this car was from the Eight Nations Hotel (the driver said it was from the Six Nations Hotel) and the owner was here (the owner had come upon hearing the news), it was different from ordinary circumstances. It seemed that the police officer could not please anyone. I told him that our time was limited and asked him to help us, so that we could leave first. He spoke to a fat, drunk foreigner, and the foreigner called us out. When we came out, the policeman also wanted to come out, perhaps to see us off, but he was scolded by the foreigner and reprimanded for bringing us there. I really wanted to hear what they said, but they seemed to not want us to stay any longer, so we left.

Taking a car around Hong Kong is just a fleeting glimpse. There are also articles about Hong Kong everywhere, so I have nothing to say. This British colony, wholly owned by China and managed for over ninety years, is clearly divided into two layers: managers and workers, British and Chinese. Under Chinese rule, it was just a desolate mountain and a small fishing port. Now, there are tall Western-style buildings, bustling streets, wide, winding paved roads, and streetcars and cars can go straight to the top of the mountain. Not to mention the universities, middle schools, and hospitals, the British have been able to manage this small place so well, and their abilities are admirable. But can't China do it? I don't know how many Chinese engineers can build these Western-style buildings and roads, and I don't know how many Chinese doctors can manage and establish such hospitals. China doesn't seem to be lacking the resources to manage these. But China never thought that a lonely, desolate island could be managed into a commercial port, and never thought that science could create a kingdom in a remote place. How many demobilized warlords and bureaucrats have been enjoying themselves in ready-made Hong Kong with tens of millions of dollars in assets, but who has thought of going somewhere else to manage another Hong Kong? After seeing Hong Kong, I feel even more that the Chinese nation only seeks to adapt to the environment and dares not resist the environment, which is a fatal injury. All politics and diplomacy...seek to adapt to the old environment and dare not create a new situation. I think it is all the inferiority of the same nation!

The ship stopped at Kowloon, and a small ferry was used to go to and from Hong Kong. There are many fishing families in Kowloon. At night, when the tide rises in the bay, they gather in groups to light up the lights and fish in the center of the bay. The fishing methods vary from house to house. They use sampans to light the lights and set up camp as the headquarters, and use small punts to cast nets. After surrounding the fish, the bow of the boat uses bamboo poles with wooden blocks to hit the water, making a sound like beating a drum, which scares the fish into the net.

In addition to fishing, they often wade into the crevices of the rocks, prying with fire sticks to search for lobsters, prawns, flower silkworms, groupers, yellow-legged wax...and some other things.

I heard that making a living in these hard ways is also difficult now. First, many of the rocky feet of the bay have been sealed off with reinforced concrete. Second, there are more and more Japanese fishing boats coming south, and they have better methods to exploit the fish in the bays.

In the dusk, when I saw a group of dark fishing boats from this large, white ConteVerde, I felt an infinite desolation in this beautiful seascape. I thought, if I were standing on that dark little boat at that time, looking at that white big ship, what would my feelings be? Isn't its huge white size a heavy oppression and fear?

But the white ship sailed away, leaving behind a little bit of light next to the mountain color, supplying the seafood for the people in those white buildings. And the ship had many more people. Mr. Chen Jitang, the commander-in-chief of an army corps, also brought his car and entourage, in the palace-like first-class cabin, saying goodbye to Hong Kong, looking far away at Guangzhou outside the mountain, and thinking about the future, what kind of thoughts would he have? I seem to see that what goes from Western-style buildings to black fishing boats is one black copper coin after another, while what goes from generals out of white big ships are tens of thousands of yellow gold pounds!

Nanhui: Expansion of Urban and Rural Telephone Service 79

The county's urban and rural telephone service is developing rapidly. The county government believes that the original regulations are no longer applicable, so it has revised the regulations on telephone charges and the interim measures for installing private telephones. The revisions have been submitted to the provincial government and approved. At the same time, a large-scale central switchboard has been installed, and the telephone exchange has been moved to the Jigu Granary, all of which have been completed. The new measures will be implemented from October 1st. The monthly fee for installing a private telephone will be five yuan, and government agencies and legal entities will be charged half price.

Kunshan: Person in Charge of Local Dialect Publication Detained 80

More than ten young people in this county, including Yan Wei, Shi Chengche, Xu Zhenya, and Sheng Xichang, jointly published the "Local Dialect Bi-Monthly." The office was located in the Bacheng Club in the Eighth District. Yan Wei and Shi Chengche were the editors, and Xu Zhenya was the publisher. The publication was issued for two issues. The content was not fair commentary but was specialized in scolding. County Magistrate Peng read the publication and was extremely angry at its intentional defamation. He immediately ordered it to be banned and instructed the Public Security Bureau to investigate. After receiving the instructions, the bureau detained Xu Zhenya and Sheng Xichang on the evening of the 23rd and summoned Yan Wei on the 24th for questioning. All were sent to the county for interrogation.

Changshu: Poor Cotton Harvest in Eastern Townships 81

In the various townships of the Fifth District of this area, most farmers grow cotton. Last year, due to unfavorable weather conditions, the harvest was sharply reduced, and it was hoped that this year would compensate. Unexpectedly, the cotton fields this autumn were damaged even more severely by a night of strong winds. The township chiefs of Donghong, Shenshi, Yongan, and Wangxian townships have jointly submitted a report to the county government, reporting the disaster situation of the cotton fields in their area. The report stated that the heavy rainstorm on August 17th knocked off almost all the cotton bolls, and the flowers could hardly bloom fully. Now it is the cotton-picking season, but there are almost no flowers to pick. For Donghong and the other three townships, the total harvest is less than 20%, which is even worse than in previous years. Therefore, they are reporting to the county government and requesting that it be forwarded to the province for review.

Suzhou: Air Defense Exhibition Opened Yesterday 82

The air defense exhibition organized by the county's air defense branch was held at the Youth Association yesterday morning (the 24th) at 9:00 AM. Special Commissioner Sun of the County Party Headquarters presided over the opening ceremony. County Magistrate Deng, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang, Instructor Deng, Adjutant Gao, and others gave speeches on the essentials of air defense and protection against poison gas. Afterwards, the exhibition was opened to the public. Among the exhibits, a huge airplane model named "Yue Jun" was the most eye-catching. Other items such as demolition bombs, gas masks, battlefield rescue photos, and oil paintings of air defense illustrations were also quite alarming and attention-grabbing. The public flocked to visit.

Wuxi: Construction of Women's Prison Housing 83

The women's prison housing of the Jiangsu Fifth Prison Branch in this county is dilapidated and overcrowded. This situation also has a great impact on the hygiene of the prisoners held in the same location. Warden Xing Yuantang, in view of this, specially raised funds to rebuild it. The dismantling began yesterday. Special Branch Director Wu Yiliang and others were assigned to supervise the construction, which is expected to be completed next month.

Changzhou: Thirteen-Year-Old Boy Hangs Himself 84

Liu Da, a resident of Beihou Street in this county, is 64 years old and has been making a living by raising horses. His wife, Yan, bore him four sons. The youngest son, Rongfa, is 13 years old and is currently studying at school. On the 19th of this month, he had a conflict with his neighbor, Jiang Quand, and went to bed after returning home. Around 3:00 PM on the 23rd, he became very agitated. His mother thought it was malaria. Around 6:00 PM, she went to his room to check on him and suddenly noticed that he was gone. She ordered her two sons to search in all directions. After an hour, they had not found him. The mother and others re-entered the room to search and found Rongfa hanging himself from a beam with a trouser belt behind the bed. After the incident occurred, it was very strange and suspicious outside, because it was indeed unheard of for a thirteen-year-old boy to hang himself.

Nantong: Township Murder Case Has Been Prosecuted 85

Dan Zhigang of Zhenchang Township, whose daughter Dan Siru married Cheng Jinming in the spring of this year. Fights broke out from time to time. On the night of the 4th of this month, Dan's father and daughter, together with Wang Jinqing and Dan Zhiyi, killed Cheng Jinming, tied his body with stones, and threw it into the river. Ten days later, the body floated up. The deceased's mother, Cheng Wang, sued the court. Prosecutor Liu examined the body and detained Dan Zhigang, Dan Siru, Dan Zhiyi, and Wang Jinqing for interrogation. Currently, all four murderers have been prosecuted for the death penalty.

Jiaxing: Murder Case in Xinfeng District 86

In Shilongqiao, Yifeng Township, Xinfeng District, Jiaxing County, Feng Jiasheng's son, Shoul (30 years old), had a conflict with Cao Jinfu and Cao Adi at the small teahouse opened by Qi Guansuo in Dalaiwei on the afternoon of the 21st due to water entering the field, resulting in a fight. Feng Shoul, who was already suffering from illness, died after being beaten. The Xinfeng District Public Security Bureau arrested the murderers Cao Jinfu and Cao Adi and sent them to the court on the 23rd. The father of the deceased has sued the court for causing death by injury. After the court sent personnel to the township to examine the body, they will schedule another interrogation. It is said that the deceased, Bi Wan, was killed by the two murderers by crushing him to death.

Business Community Asks for Exemption from Levy 87

Jiaxing merchants believe that the Zhejiang Provincial Government has changed the method of collecting grain reserves, changing it to annual fundraising without restrictions. Furthermore, merchants' grain reserves are assessed based on their business tax, with one-third of the business tax amount being levied, which is difficult to bear. The Xinzha Town Chamber of Commerce, under the county's jurisdiction, has sent a telegram to the Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce, requesting that they strongly advocate to the Executive Yuan and the Provincial Government for exemption from implementation, in order to alleviate the difficulties of Suzhou merchants.

Letter to the Editor 88

The company that was fined was Xingji Tugaohang (which is now closed). The Sanxin Tugaohang mentioned in your newspaper was not fined. We are still afraid of misunderstandings from the outside world, so we are sending this letter to request a correction. Sincerely, Jiading Sanxin Tugaohang.

Local News

Municipal Government: Protests Japanese Military Deployment Beyond Borders. Submitted a Written Protest to the Japanese Consulate General Yesterday Morning. Ordered the Public Security Bureau to Protect Overseas Chinese and Assist in Apprehending Murderers the Night Before. Director Cai Decides to Assist the Police in Strictly Apprehending the Murderers Yesterday 89

Central News Agency reports that after the incident on the afternoon of the 23rd at 8:00 PM in which Japanese sailor Tagang was shot and killed by rioters near Haining Road and Wusong Road in the Hongkou Concession, the Japanese Naval Headquarters considered the situation serious. To search for the murderers and protect overseas Chinese, it immediately sent Marine Corps soldiers to deploy strictly in the concession and Zhabei, setting up sentries and checking pedestrians. The municipal government believes that although the Japanese Navy's actions are said to be for the protection of overseas Chinese, they concern the sovereignty of this country and cannot be agreed to. Regarding the protection of overseas Chinese, the municipal government has already ordered its subordinates to handle it strictly, and the Japanese Navy's actions are unnecessary. Therefore, Mayor Wu submitted a written protest to the Japanese Consulate General yesterday morning, requesting that the Japanese Marine Corps sent to the urban area be withdrawn immediately to avoid misunderstandings.

The municipal government issued an instruction to the Public Security Bureau at 9:30 PM on the 23rd, stating: "It has been reported that a Japanese sailor was suddenly attacked and shot by rioters near Haining Road and Wusong Road in the Public Concession, resulting in one death and two injuries. Although this case occurred within the Public Concession, in order to maintain the city's public security, it is urgent to find ways to apprehend the perpetrators and bring them to justice. Since there are many Japanese residents within the jurisdiction of this city, we should continue to be vigilant and protect them strictly to avoid negligence. We hereby order the bureau to comply with and implement this order." Public Security Bureau Director Cai Jinjun spent the night at the bureau working, directing subordinate officers and police to be especially vigilant and investigate the perpetrators, and stepping up the protection of Japanese residents due to the incident in which Japanese sailor Tagang was killed in the corner of Haining Road and Wusong Road in the Public Concession the night before. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, he convened a meeting at the bureau with the chiefs of various branches, stations, and teams, as well as senior officials of the bureau, to discuss the following measures: (1) Assist the Public Concession Police Department in strictly investigating the perpetrators in order to solve the case as soon as possible; (2) In the Zhabei area, the residential areas of Japanese residents should be strictly enforced by the chiefs of the relevant branches and stations in accordance with the previously issued measures for the protection of overseas Chinese, and the inspection department should send personnel to inspect at any time to prevent laxity; (3) After the occurrence of this case, residents in the Zhabei area will inevitably be panicked. The relevant police stations should inform each household that the bureau is absolutely responsible for local public security, and they should live and work in peace and not disturb each other or relocate, causing losses. All subordinates have been notified to comply with these instructions.

Japanese Marine Corps Withdrawn from Zhabei Area Last Night 90

Central News Agency reports that after the incident in which Japanese sailors were shot by rioters at the intersection of Haining Road and Wusong Road the night before, the Japanese Marine Corps, upon hearing the news, immediately deployed strictly around the incident site, on North Sichuan Road, from Laobazi Road to Jiangwan Road, and gradually expanded the area. In the Zhabei area, from Tiantong'an Road Tiantong'an Station to the east to East Sports Association Road, south to West Baoxing Road Yokohama Bridge, west to Yokohama River as the boundary, and north to Baziqiao, Shuidian Road, and Guangdong Middle School, sentries were densely deployed along the road, carrying guns and live ammunition, and strictly checking pedestrians. The situation was quite serious. By 6:00 PM last night, the team had been gradually withdrawn. There was no trace of Japanese troops at Tongji Road and Yokohama Road. Our Public Security Bureau also exercised its duties as usual. Only near the 63 Huayuan Garden had not been completely withdrawn. At the junction of the Chinese concession where North Sichuan Road crosses the border to build roads, the number of Japanese Marine Corps outposts had also decreased.

Details of the Shooting of Japanese Sailors in Hongkou Yesterday. The Japanese Side's Attitude Is Extremely Serious. The Result of Negotiations with the Police Department: Three Suspects Transferred for Temporary Detention. To Be Sent to Court Today for Hearing 91

After three Japanese sailors were shot in the jurisdiction of the Hongkou Police Department of the Public Concession at the intersection of Wusong Road and Haining Road the night before, the Hongkou area was immediately tense. Almost all of the Japanese Marine Corps were deployed for defense, checking pedestrians with extreme strictness. The Police Department, fearing further accidents, urgently ordered all police detectives to patrol back and forth in coordination with those on duty. Starting yesterday, the entire reserve team was also ordered to report for duty to prevent any eventuality. All incident sites and junctions with the Chinese concession, from Bazhi Road to Jiangwan Road, were guarded by armed Japanese Marine Corps, and inspections were even stricter. However, the authority of Chinese police officers was not obstructed. Inside the Japanese elementary school at Arui Lane on North Sichuan Road and the Taoyue Dancing Ground at the intersection of Baoxing Road, branch offices of the Marine Corps have now been set up. The Japanese elementary schools in the Hongkou area have been temporarily closed starting yesterday by order of the Japanese Residents Association. Military vehicles and patrol motorcycles of the Marine Corps traveled frequently along North Sichuan Road to Jiangwan Road. Therefore, although the residents there witnessed the statement and announcement of Japanese Marine Corps Commander Kondo Eiketsu, they could not help but feel uneasy.

Three Suspects Handed Over to the Police Department Yesterday

As for the three suspects who were taken to the headquarters by the Marine Corps after the incident, one was Zhang Ronghe, from Taizhou, 21 years old, a peddler living at No. 8 Ruikang Lane, Disui Road. During a house-to-house search, he was arrested because Zhang happened to be wearing a tattered Western-style shirt, which was considered suspicious. There were also two brothers, named Ma Yongcai, from Jiading, 30 years old, and Ma Yongnian, 27 years old, who lived together at AC No. 9 Ruiji Lane, Dongjiaxing Road. During the day, both brothers worked at the China Printing House at No. 24, Lane 406, Shanhai Pass Road. The night before, the brothers finished work and walked home. When they passed Wusong Road, the incident happened to occur, and the military and police were searching. The two brothers suddenly saw the crowd gathering and the traffic stopping. Fearing involvement, they turned around and returned, and their steps were inevitably a little hurried. Unexpectedly, they were considered to be evading inspection and therefore arrested. The three were taken to the Marine Corps headquarters. After a night of detention and negotiations with the Police Department, Ma and his brother were first sent back to the Police Department at 12:30 PM yesterday. After further negotiations by the Police Department, Zhang Ronghe was sent back to the Police Department at around 7:30 PM last night. After questioning by senior officials of the Police Department, they were temporarily detained. It is reported that they will be sent to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation this morning.

Two Guns Found in Two Places

Starting at midnight yesterday morning, the entire police force of the Police Department checked people entering the jurisdiction. West Police Officer No. 143 of No. 3 Pier, while patrolling near Xiyuqing Lane, Haining Road, suddenly found a .38 caliber pistol on the side of the road, with four bullets in the chamber. Autumn Native Products Festival Opens Yesterday. Expanded Publicity Promotes Native Products. Helps Economic Construction Movement 92

The Chinese Native Products Promotion Association stipulated that yesterday (the 24th) to the 30th would be the Autumn Native Products Festival. It has notified members everywhere and issued a declaration, asking everyone to promote native products uniformly. Yesterday was the opening of the Autumn Festival. The reporter went to the association on Xiafei Road to inquire about the meaning of the Native Products Festival. It is said that our country has many social programs, the meaning of which is only to provide the public with leisure, social interaction, consumption, and superstitious living opportunities. Therefore, everything that is eaten, worn, traveled, lived, and used, such as copper, iron, tin, wood, lacquer, and earth utensils, as well as native cloth and fruits, are all necessities for the festival. Social festivals are indeed the most prosperous days for buying native products. Since the failure of the Opium War, imperialists have continued to invade constantly. Under the coercion and inducement of foreign goods dumping and customs smuggling, all the items we need have gradually been transformed from native products into foreign goods. The psychology of foreign goods dumping purchasers, foreign goods manipulate the Chinese market, so leisure festivals have become places for selling foreign goods, in social festivals, it seems dishonorable not to wear foreign clothes or foreign goods, in banquets for guests, it seems embarrassing not to have wine and Western food, so native products are rejected from the market by foreign goods, and customs super-entry figures increase day by day, economic blood is also depleted day by day, after this kind of poison seed, the countryside went bankrupt, the crowd went unemployed, and the festivals that have been transformed by our society had to be changed. The value of the festival had to be lowered. The people of this association want to restore the meaning of the festival, increase the value of the festival, make the festival a competition of native products, make the festival a native products festival, make the festival have the determination to improve native products, make holidaymakers develop the habit of using native products, make holidaymakers create a self-rescue movement that unites production and sales, make holidaymakers create a lasting national economic construction movement, make holidaymakers create a self-governing, self-sufficient, self-defensive national self-conscious movement, So we stipulated that March 10 to 17 would be the Spring Native Products Festival, June 17 to 23 would be the Summer Native Products Festival, September 24 to 30 would be the Autumn Native Products Festival, and December 18 to 25 would be the Winter Native Products Festival. Now that it is the Autumn Native Products Festival, and the National Economic Construction Movement has begun to be active, the members of this association are working especially hard on this in order to fulfill their national duties.

Newly Appointed Gansu Provincial Finance Director Chen Duan Flies to Gansu This Morning 93

Xin Xin News Agency reports that Chen Duan (Xin Ming), the newly appointed Director of Finance of Gansu Province, has been in Shanghai for several days, contacting financial and industrial circles about investment matters, and there are already signs of progress. He is scheduled to fly to Gansu this morning on a Eurasian Aviation Company plane to take office. Chen met with reporters yesterday and issued a speech on the plan to reorganize the finances of Gansu Province, which is divided into the following:

Gansu Provincial Finance

Chen said that the finances of Gansu Province, after the previous Director Zhu formulated a balance plan, should not exceed the budget. However, due to a small part of the bandits making trouble, there were temporary special expenditures. In the future, when the banditry is calmed, it can be gradually restored. The total revenue part of this year's budget is more than 9 million yuan, and the expenditure part is 11 million yuan, which has been approved by the Ministry of Finance. According to the budget situation, the annual shortfall is 2 million yuan. If we engage in increasing revenue and reducing expenditure, the financial future can be expected to be balanced.

Reorganization Plan

The reorganization plan is nothing more than increasing revenue and reducing expenditure, but in terms of palliative treatment it is reducing expenditure, and in terms of fundamental treatment it is increasing revenue. Because Gansu Province is located in a remote area, many products have not yet been developed, so there is more hope for cultivating tax sources. The first step that needs to be carried out urgently is the opening up of transportation routes, so that Gansu's special products such as woolen textiles can be transported out, and cotton textiles from other provinces can also be transported in successively. After the necessary items inside and outside the province are circulated, the production and construction can also be gradually increased. Secondly, we should also strive to carry out water conservancy construction, so that agricultural production can reduce the losses caused by drought. At the same time, we hope that people from all walks of life inside and outside the province will help develop various special products. In the future, production will develop, financial will revive, and there will be hope.

Contact Investment

According to Chen, while in Shanghai, he had private contacts with financial and industrial leaders in this city, asking them to invest in Gansu Province, develop various special products, and develop industries. He has now received permission from the leaders, and in the near future, an inspection team will be organized to go to Gansu for inspection, and then plans will be gradually implemented. The secretary Wang Lingxiao has already gone to arrange things. The company includes two finance department staff members Xue Minong and Xu Haoyuan.

The Shanghai Municipal Committee for Raising Funds to Purchase Airplanes as a Gift to the Government in Commemoration of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Fiftieth Birthday, held a meeting yesterday (the 24th) at 5:00 PM at the Baxian (Eight Immortals) gathering of various organizations, to discuss expanding the publicity campaign for purchasing airplanes to celebrate the birthday. Attendees included Zhang Yichen from the First Special District Citizens' Federation, Xian Shi from the Zhigong Party, Hu Fengxiang from the Local Association, Wang Boxuan from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Zhu Boyuan from the Municipal General Labor Union, Zhou Xuexiang from the Municipal Farmers' Association, Zhang Huijun from the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Workers' Union, Feng Zhongda from the Municipal Library, Li Dachao from the Airplane Purchase Commemoration Committee, and representatives from over twenty other organizations. He has worked tirelessly day and night, struggling amid internal and external troubles, enduring hardships and complaints without hesitation. Finally, he has achieved authority and virtue, suppressed the Red bandits, and completed unification, allowing the people to live in peace and the government to become more transparent. His great achievements are admired by all. Since Shanghai began raising funds to purchase airplanes to celebrate the birthday, it has received enthusiastic support from all sectors of society. It is estimated that 600,000 yuan will be received by the end of the month. All entertainment venues and broadcasting stations will promote the significance of purchasing airplanes to celebrate the birthday. Slogans will be posted in prominent locations in all city agencies, organizations, companies, shops, and along major roads, and other powerful written propaganda will be used to attract the attention of all sectors of society, to recognize the significance of purchasing airplanes to celebrate the birthday, and to encourage greater participation in donations, so that those who have already donated will contribute more private funds, and those who have not donated will enthusiastically donate, so as to achieve the original goal of raising one million yuan, purchasing ten airplanes, and presenting them as a gift. It is hoped that important organizations and enthusiastic individuals in the city will provide powerful support. Furthermore, in order to expand the publicity for purchasing airplanes to celebrate the birthday, the committee has sent letters to the authorities of the Public and French Concessions, requesting their assistance in posting slogans in shops throughout the city. The two Concessions sent representatives to discuss the matter and agreed to cooperate. Yesterday, the committee also received a reply from the Public Works Department stating that slogans for purchasing airplanes to celebrate the birthday could be posted at the entrances of shops.

Banking and Finance Industry: Preparing to Implement Income Tax; Gao Bingfang and Cui Weiwo Returned to Beijing Last Night 97

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the income tax on securities deposit interest will be implemented on October 1st. Gao Bingfang, director of the Central Direct Tax Preparatory Office, and others returned to Beijing last night. The Bankers' Association will hold a meeting tomorrow to prepare everything, and the Money Dealers' Association will hold a meeting today to study the matter. Details are as follows:

Gao Bingfang and Others Returned to Beijing Last Night

After arriving in Shanghai from Beijing, Gao Bingfang, director of the Central Direct Tax Preparatory Office, Liang Hejun, deputy director, and Cui Weiwo, secretary, signed contracts with the Central Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau to collect income tax on their behalf, and negotiated with the banking and finance industry on the collection of income tax on securities deposit interest. They also hosted Shanghai journalists to report on the progress of the central government's implementation of income tax. Deputy Director Liang Hejun had already returned to Beijing the night before, and Director Gao Bingfang and Secretary Cui Weiwo further discussed various procedures for collecting income tax with the banking sector yesterday, deciding to implement it as scheduled on October 1st, and then took the Shanghai-Beijing night express train back to Beijing at 11:00 PM last night.

The Bankers' Association, the Shanghai Banking Association, requested the government to implement the income tax on securities deposit interest and other income taxes simultaneously on New Year's Day next year. After Deputy Director Liang of the Central Direct Tax Preparatory Office explained to the banks, they are now preparing to implement it on the 11th. The association has compiled the opinions of banking societies and various banks on income tax, totaling more than ten articles, and has already mimeographed them. It is scheduled to hold an executive committee meeting tomorrow (Saturday) at 4:00 PM, and invite representatives from member banks to attend and discuss the matter together. After the opinions are approved, they will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for adoption. These opinions are all related to procedural issues of income tax, such as avoiding double taxation, etc.

Henan Provincial Government Borrows 600,000 Yuan from the Banking Sector 101

The Kaifeng branches of the Bank of Communications and other banks provide loans to invest in production and construction projects. The Henan Provincial Government, in order to carry out local production and construction projects, borrowed 600,000 yuan from the Kaifeng branches of the Bank of Communications and other banks to organize a production and construction association to promote investment. The loan has been approved by the head office. The reporter investigated the purpose and methods of the loan as follows:

Purpose of the Loan

The Henan Provincial Government, in order to promote production and construction, repeatedly contacted the Kaifeng banking sector, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Shanghai banks. As a result, it was decided that the banks would jointly lend 600,000 yuan. The provincial government and the banking industry would jointly form a production and construction committee to handle investment matters. The purpose of the loan is allocated as follows: (1) Agricultural development and water conservancy: 150,000 yuan (including 60,000 yuan for siphon pipe expenses); (2) Silk reeling and dyeing factory: 100,000 yuan; (3) Oil pressing plant: 100,000 yuan; (4) Paper mill: 150,000 yuan; (5) Various contingency fees: 100,000 yuan. Totaling 600,000 yuan.

Repayment Method

The method of repaying the principal and interest of the loan and sharing the profits has also been decided by both parties: (1) The sale price of reclaimed land will be the first fund, and the surplus from the business will be the second fund; (2) If the business has no surplus within two years, the income from the provincial long-distance telephone bureau will be used to pay interest. If the interest payable in the first year is insufficient, the shortfall will be added to the interest payable in the following year, and paid together from the surplus in the following year. The above methods have been reported to the Shanghai head office by the banks for approval, and have been approved by the Henan Provincial Government meeting. A contract has been signed to establish a production and construction association and begin distributing the funds to carry out the projects in sequence.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Notifies Fishing Vessel Industry to Return Overcharged Fees 104

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce yesterday notified the Shanghai Fishing Vessel Industry Association that it had previously received a request from the association to promptly order the return of overcharged fees, and attached opinions on the case of abolishing the middlemen. It has ordered the resident supervisor of the Shanghai Fish Market to report jointly with the council, stating that (1) there are no clear legal provisions for the item of "uplift fee." In the past, the relationship between cargo owners and workers was close and frequent, so it was common to give some rewards to show consideration, but whether to pay or not was entirely voluntary by the cargo owner and could not be forcibly demanded. The association has already made a decision on this matter. However, once this practice started, it almost became a bad example, and disputes arose from time to time, which was contrary to the original intention. In order to eliminate disputes, the association had already informed the fish market to strictly correct it. Now, it is ordered to reiterate to the association that, in addition to the fees stipulated in the regulations, no other unfair fees should be charged and all bad practices should be abolished. The "uplift fee" is undoubtedly one of the unfair fees, and there is no objection to abolishing it. The association has been instructed to inform the market to order the unloaders to comply and return all previously overcharged amounts. (2) The sea fish unloaders intend to modify Article 1 of the operating regulations, and the purpose is nothing more than to charge an extra share of service fees. However, the article has not been approved. Before the amendment, the association had informed the market to order the unloaders to operate in accordance with the original regulations. However, the unloaders were too hasty and did not wait for the amendment of the article before arbitrarily overcharging. The association has repeatedly warned them, but the unloaders have been slow to comply. It is ordered to strictly implement Article 52 of the operating regulations and return the previously overcharged service fees in full within three days of receiving the document. If the unloaders violate the regulations again, the market should propose punishment measures. It is reported that the unloaders have returned all previously overcharged fees in accordance with the ministry's order. This case can be considered closed. (3) The opinions of the unloaders submitted by the fishing vessel association may not be entirely true. Since the establishment of the fish market, the setting up of unloaders in the process of centralized fish trading has been an indispensable tool. Whether there is a need for unloaders to exist in the future is another question, and it should be determined according to the needs of the environment. In addition to the instructions, this is a notification.

Dutch East Indies Abolishes Restrictions on Native Cloth Imports; Xu Tinglie Informs National Trade Bureau of the Process 105

The International Trade Bureau of this city received a letter from Xu Tinglie, the commercial commissioner of our country stationed in the Dutch East Indies, stating the agreement of the Dutch East Indies government to abolish the import restriction clauses of native cloth and the process. The original letter states: "To whom it may concern, in accordance with letters No. 627 and 1109 of April 24th and July 7th, I have replied to you on May 18th and August 7th respectively. Now, I will send you the results of the investigation and the unanimous efforts of the Dutch East Indies authorities in consultation. After receiving the first letter from your bureau reporting the situation of native cloth exporting to the Dutch East Indies, I conducted a detailed investigation of the political and business circles, such as the cotton lan (Mepan, Plembang, Pemgkal Pinang), Jambi, and Penang, and discussed everything in detail with the chambers of commerce there. According to the relevant commercial groups, the information can confirm the situation of the Shanghai Native Cloth Industry Association's call for the Dutch East Indies to restrict the import of native cloth. According to the report from the Batavia Cisis Import Bureau (the agency to which the Shanghai Native Cloth Industry Association sent five small samples), it can further prove the difficulties faced by native cloth merchants. According to the bureau, the first to fourth samples (i.e., Lin Dacheng, An Chun, Da You, Fang Fu) belong to tax number 257 and are not subject to import restrictions. The fifth sample (Xia Zhuang cloth) belongs to tax number 1575 and, because it exceeds the maximum weight limit, cannot be imported in theory. However, according to the regulations of the Ministry of Economic Affairs, samples of the same quality as the fifth sample are not subject to this regulation. In other words, native cloth belonging to number 157 in terms of weight does not need to follow the 135 kg standard. Under the above circumstances, it is necessary for me to make formal representations to the highest-level authorities. Therefore, I tried to draw the attention of the acting director of the bureau to the decline of the industry. Although the director made concessions, it was still not entirely satisfactory. Last week, when I was in Batavia, I visited the acting minister of the Ministry of Economy of the Dutch East Indies government to discuss the difficulties faced by the restriction of native cloth. After repeated consultations, the acting minister agreed to make concessions. All kinds of native cloth (including the five cloth samples sent by your bureau and the Shanghai Native Cloth Industry Association) can be imported regardless of their weight, length, width, and the number of threads per seven square millimeters, as long as they can be sold in the Dutch East Indies market. The necessary procedure is only to apply for an import permit. Existing import merchants can obtain the permit as usual, while newly established merchants must go through reasonable consideration by the authorities. Now that the Dutch East Indies government is willing to give preferential treatment to native cloth importers, our country should formulate laws and regulations to implement a close approach. The first two points (increasing the import quota to show preferential treatment and revising the weight, length, and width restrictions) of the three points requested by the Shanghai Native Cloth Industry Association have now been achieved. The third point is slightly ambiguous, and it can be interpreted in two ways: (1) Reducing customs duties; (2) Reducing permit fees. (1) Reducing customs duties: The Dutch East Indies government's import tax on cotton cloth is 12% ad valorem and 50% surtax. It is not possible to modify the tariff. Therefore, it should be understood that because the value of native cloth is quite low, the import tax collected is also relatively small. (2) Reducing permit fees: The permit fee is 3 Dutch cents per hundred yards. The minimum fee paid for cotton cloth is 6.5 Dutch cents, which is only 5 Dutch cents difference. Even if native cloth can use the lowest fee, I believe that the small amount is not what the Shanghai Native Cloth Industry Association is fighting for. The points determined by the Minister of Economy have been enough to remove all obstacles to the transport of Chinese native cloth to the Netherlands. It is hoped that the Chinese native cloth industry will not only recover its lost market but also open up new markets. Sincerely, Xu Tinglie, Commercial Commissioner stationed in the Dutch East Indies, to the Director of the International Trade Bureau."
