Jiangsu Chamber of Commerce Federation Vigorously Strives for the Jurisdiction of Shengsi Islands to Belong to Jiangsu; Sends Separate Telegrams to the Executive Yuan and Ministry of Interior, Insisting on Determining the Border According to the Original Boundary 106

The Shengsi Islands, located in the outer sea of Jiangsu Province, have been in dispute for more than a year since the Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association of Zhejiang Province proposed that they be placed under the jurisdiction of Zhejiang Province. Recently, the Executive Yuan convened a review meeting, and the representative of Zhejiang Province proposed a new boundary, 30 degrees 53 minutes north latitude, which would include the Shengsi Islands and the entire sea area of Jinshan and Fengxian Counties. Representatives of the chambers of commerce of Chongming and other counties believed that this would seriously harm the fishing industry and economy of Jiangsu Province. The fifth membership congress of the Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation passed a resolution to send separate telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Interior, requesting that the border be determined according to the original boundary. The original telegram is recorded below: "To Premier Chiang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, We, the [undersigned] association, held the fifth membership congress on the 20th of this month. The Chongming and other chambers of commerce proposed that Zhejiang Province is encroaching on Jiangsu's territory in the outer sea, and the Shengsi Islands, a mere fishing area, have a huge impact on Jiangsu's fishing industry and economy. We request that separate telegrams be sent to the central Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Interior to vigorously strive for the cause. This was immediately brought to the meeting for discussion. It was generally agreed that the maritime islands of Jiangsu and Zhejiang were clearly demarcated during the Kangxi period of the Qing Dynasty, with monuments erected to protect them forever. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, the Jiangsu Provincial Government proposed to delineate the boundaries of the fishing area due to fishery disputes. The case was then negotiated by the representatives of the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang and the two ministries of Interior and Commerce, and a slight revision was made, but the original boundary was still approved, and it was also approved by the Zhejiang Provincial Government Committee. Recently, the Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association of Zhejiang Province suddenly proposed that the Shengsi Islands be归劃ed to Zhejiang, which has been repeatedly opposed by Jiangsu Province. Now, it is heard that the representative of Zhejiang Province has proposed a new boundary line at the review meeting of the Executive Yuan, which is 30 degrees 53 minutes north latitude, which will include the Shengsi Islands and the entire sea area of Jinshan and Fengxian. This will seriously harm the fishing industry and economy of Jiangsu Province. We should present it to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Interior separately, clearly order the determination of the maritime boundary between Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and delineate it according to the original boundary, in order to prevent disputes. It was resolved and recorded in the minutes. In addition to sending separate telegrams, we hereby report the situation to your esteemed Yuan (Ministry) for review and approval, and grant a clear order to determine the border according to the original boundary for public convenience. Sincerely, The Presidium of the Fifth Membership Congress of the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation, Yu Xiaochuan, Cheng Ganqing, Lan Bohua, Qian Sunqing, Wang Xiaoting."

Opposing Joint Government-Business Operation: Tobacco Leaf Industry to Petition 107

Due to the large-scale production of handmade cigarettes in Shanghai, which has a significant impact on national tax revenue, the Ministry of Finance is implementing control over tobacco leaves, setting up a buying and selling agency, which will be jointly operated by the government and merchants, with a capital of 500,000 to 1 million yuan. The tax authorities have convened a meeting of tobacco leaf merchants. The Shanghai Tobacco Leaf Industry Association supports the central government's control, but believes that the joint operation of the buying and selling agency will cut off the livelihood of the industry. It has requested the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association to forward the request to the central government for a change. Yesterday, the association again sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, requesting the two ministries of Finance and Industry to take into account both national taxes and the livelihood of merchants, abolish the joint government-business operation proposal, and find another appropriate method. It is reported that the association will send representatives to Beijing to petition if necessary.

American Warships to Return to Shanghai in Succession 111

The "Renlu Bao" reports that at the beginning of October, the various ships of the American Asiatic Fleet, while sailing south from North China back to the Philippines, will pass through Shanghai in succession. The first to arrive will be the cruiser USS Augusta, carrying Admiral Murfin, who will stay in Shanghai for a month. The other ships will stay for periods ranging from three weeks to a month. The USS Augusta is the flagship of the fleet, carrying 500 soldiers. It was docked in Qingdao for a long time this summer and is currently in Qinhuangdao. Admiral Murfin is currently in Beiping inspecting the U.S. Embassy guard and handling other official business. Before coming to Shanghai, he will also make a trip to Yantai. Following the USS Augusta, the next ship to arrive in Shanghai will be the Black Hawk, the mother ship of the U.S. destroyer squadron in Liaodong. The squadron has a total of eleven ships, but only nine sailed north this summer. Now all of them will arrive in Shanghai, carrying a total of 2,000 officers and sailors. There will also be six submarines and the submarine tender USS Canopus, carrying 700 officers and sailors, which will also arrive. It is also reported that four minesweepers and the admiral's yacht USS Isabel will also visit here. In addition, there are several American warships originally docked in the Huangpu River. Therefore, it is expected that the waters of Shanghai will be very lively in October. The owners of various shops, pubs, and entertainment venues are all overjoyed at this news.

Leaders of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Representatives of the Paper Industry Petition: Requesting Exemption from Transport Permit for Paper Products 112

The Shanghai Paper Industry Association, feeling difficulties in the transport and sale of various types of paper after the Ministry of Finance revised the list of goods subject to inspection for imported goods, specially appointed nine people, including Liu Minzhai and Zhang Peizhen, to petition in Beijing last night under the leadership of Ke Ganzhen, a standing committee member of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Ge Jiezhen, the director. The petition is recorded as follows:

Letter from the Paper Industry Association to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: We respectfully write to inform you that since the Ministry of Finance revised the list of goods subject to inspection for imported goods, the three words "cigarette paper" have been changed to "various types of paper," including cigarette paper. We are experiencing difficulties everywhere in the transport and sale of paper goods. It is permissible to disassemble and sell paper in small quantities, but the permit application process is cumbersome and cannot be completed on the same day, resulting in subsequent batches of goods being unable to continue to be transported and sold. In addition, domestically produced machine-made paper is also occasionally wrongly detained in other ports. Furthermore, there are discrepancies between the methods of the Railway Bureau and the Customs for domestically produced handmade paper from Zhejiang, Fujian, Jiangxi, and Anhui. The Customs believes that there is no need to apply for a transport and sales permit, while the Railway Bureau believes that a permit must be obtained before release, resulting in the complete cessation of goods that were previously transported by rail, causing considerable losses and deep suffering. We have learned that cigarette paper in Shanghai is handled by cigarette companies and import firms. Although cigarette paper belongs to the paper category, it is not sold by the members of our association and therefore does not fall within the scope of the paper industry. Since rampant smuggling in North China, tax-evading cigarette paper has been smuggled into Shanghai in large quantities under the background of the Eastern Hebei Anti-Communist Autonomous Council, evading a considerable amount of paper and cigarette taxes, which should be strictly investigated to protect national tax revenue. As for other paper, no smuggled goods have been found in Shanghai. Examining the reasons, foreign paper is inexpensive, has a low tax rate, and the goods are bulky and not easily smuggled. The facts are all there for investigation. Our association recently received a joint request from members to forward a request to the Ministry of Finance to maintain the original proposal and abolish the inspection of paper in order to alleviate suffering. Based on this, the Executive Supervisory Committee of our association passed a resolution on September 18 to appoint committee members Liu Minzhai, Zhang Peizhen, Zhang Ruikang, Xia Kangmin, Lu Muhan, Jin Jianxiang, Zhuo Nianci, Zhu Kangnian, Fan Xiling, and others as representatives to go to Beijing with the representatives of your association at 1:00 PM on September 23 to petition the Ministry of Finance to abolish the inspection of all types of paper other than cigarette paper in order to maintain business. We hereby respectfully inform your association and request your approval to send personnel to Beijing to lead the petition in order to promote public welfare.

Chamber of Commerce Submission: Submission regarding the matter of petition (omitted). Upon investigation, handmade native goods are not included in the scope of the domestic goods transportation and sales licenses stipulated by your ministry. The customs follows the orders of your ministry and deems that no license is required, while the railway bureau holds a different opinion and often creates difficulties, which disrespects the orders of the competent inspection agency and causes merchants to feel at a loss. We have already submitted a telegram on the 12th of this month requesting verification and instructions. As for the association's request that the types of paper to be inspected should remain as stipulated in the initial decision, limited to cigarette paper only, and that other ordinary paper should not be included, this is purely based on the history of smuggling and infiltration and the absence of other ordinary paper involvement, as the basis for this petition. This is purely a matter of fact. Your ministry has detailed reports on the types of smuggled goods seized by customs authorities in various regions, which can easily corroborate the information provided by the association. Considering that the customs tariff lists imported foreign goods reaching over six hundred and seventy items, the current determination of about twenty types of imported goods to be inspected is based on whether there is large-scale smuggling of those items. If, as the association states, smuggled goods from North China infiltrating this city, except for cigarette paper, and no other ordinary paper has been found, then the non-inclusion of those paper types in the list of imported goods subject to inspection is consistent with other foreign goods. Based on the above, we respectfully recommend that representatives Ke Ganzhen and Jiezhen be dispatched to prepare documents for the petition, together with the representatives sent by the association, to respectfully consult with your ministry, present everything in person, and request your approval to handle the matter as requested, which would be in the public interest.

Response from the Ministry of Finance: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance yesterday stating: "Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce reviewed, we have received your telegram, since it is claimed that the form and types of the said handmade native paper are completely different from foreign machine-made paper, the request to be exempted from the transportation and sales license can be approved as requested. We will instruct the Customs Service to notify the General Tax Office, Ministry of Finance (Official Seal)."

Brokers Using Transaction Orders: Ministry of Industry Sends Letter to Joint Association for Explanation 113

The Ministry of Industry yesterday sent a letter to the Exchange Joint Association, stating: "Regarding the case of restricting exchange brokers from legally using transaction orders, this ministry previously stated that the case concerns the judiciary. After consulting with the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Judicial Administration replied that it has ordered the Shanghai court to handle such exchange dispute cases where transaction orders are not used. Except for cases where their trading behavior is deemed legally invalid or subject to revocation, the brokers should first be ordered to reissue the transaction orders before being tried." Accordingly, the method of ordering the reissuance of transaction orders before trial, as replied, does impose a certain restriction on brokers who do not use transaction orders. However, the Exchange Law clearly stipulates that the transaction order should be made by the exchange and issued to both parties for signing. If they are allowed to reissue transaction orders after a dispute arises, it would contradict the intent of the Exchange Law. In order to effectively restrict illegal trading, the court should, in the event of broker trading disputes, order the reissuance only when the transaction has been legally registered and recognized by the exchange but the order has not yet been made. As for brokers who illegally do not use transaction orders, or whose transaction orders are not made by a legal exchange, their trading behavior should be deemed legally invalid, and there is no need to order the reissuance of transaction orders. After this ministry and the Ministry of Finance jointly sent a letter to the Ministry of Judicial Administration for clarification and handling, we received a reply stating, "The previous letter from this ministry stating that brokers should first be ordered to reissue transaction orders before trial refers to legal transactions. If the court deems the trading behavior to be legally invalid or revocable, it should be handled separately according to law, and there is no need to order the reissuance of transaction orders. In addition to ordering the Shanghai Higher Court Second and Third Branch to inform, please be informed accordingly." The ministry hereby notifies the association to immediately inform all exchanges and broker associations. This is a special notice.

Association of Bicycle Manufacturers and Dealers Requests Department for Relief of Freight: Five Points of Difficulty 114

The Shanghai Bicycle Manufacturers and Dealers Association, stating that freight transport has stagnated since the Ministry of Finance implemented inspections on bicycles and accessories under customs orders, has specially petitioned the Ministry of Finance for relief. The reasons for the difficulty, summarized into five points, are: (1) Bicycles and accessories are diverse, mostly purchased in batches and sold in installments. Considering just one bicycle, over thirty types of verification and tax payment documents are required. When merchants in other ports purchase, there are at least ten types and up to hundreds, and the busyness can be imagined. (2) Imported accessories may be several types or even dozens of types included in one tax payment document. For example, chains, sprockets, and steel wires are imported and assembled in one box with one document, which cannot be separated. If Company A purchases a dozen chains and they are being transported by customs and have not yet been returned, and Company B purchases sprockets and Company C purchases steel wires, they cannot be transported immediately. Furthermore, small accessories such as screws, springs, and small rubber parts are sold in batches of hundreds of packages, hundreds of dozens, or thousands of gross, often starting with one package, half a dozen, or several gross, and distributed to dozens or hundreds of households. However, customs restricts each tax payment document to at least one box, making it impossible to separate them for verification, which is practically impossible. (3) It takes a long time for customs to issue transport permits, and they stop working on Sundays. Bicycle merchants conduct business every day, and there must be dozens of shipments for export, resulting in backlog and stagnation, which has a significant impact. If customers in other ports purchase one or two bicycles for their own use, or small businesses purchase a small number of parts, and carry them with them for same-day return trips, they are completely stalled because the transport permits cannot be obtained on the same day. (4) When bicycle merchants report accessories for export, sometimes a portion is foreign goods and a portion is domestic goods, packed in the same box. Foreign goods must be verified and licensed, and domestic goods must be individually licensed by the manufacturers for domestic goods transportation and sales. One box of goods must wait until all transport permits are obtained before it can be shipped, which takes a long time. There are also cases where one type of domestic goods transport permit is obtained, but the other types of permits have already expired. (5) Military and commercial entities do not directly order goods but purchase accessories from other businesses to assemble complete bicycles. When selling, they must collect tax payment documents from other businesses in order to obtain transport permits, which is cumbersome and practically impossible. We have laid out the situation of the bicycle industry and request relief. However, it is understood that the association has previously sent representatives to the customs authorities to request convenience. The customs has now approved concessions, such as issuing certificates by the association for domestic bicycle accessories and complete bicycles for military use, for the purpose of obtaining transportation and sales licenses to facilitate matters. As for the association's enthusiasm for assisting in the detection of smuggling, it is actively underway. The association has distributed charters, voluntary letters, guarantee letters, and registration application forms to the industry within three days to find suitable guarantors to be submitted to the association for safekeeping, and has registered the inventory, while simultaneously reporting to the General Smuggling Association for record-keeping. The industry must register with the customs to obtain licenses, and has been notified to pay attention to avoid penalties.

New Clues in the Double Corpse Case at the Hongkou Women's Hospital: Zhang Wenhua's Rickshaw Puller Apprehended; Rickshaw Puller is Liang Meiyu's Younger Brother; Account of the Case Still Untruthful and Incomplete 116

Inside the Hongkou Women's Hospital at 290 Zhaofeng Road, Hongkou, this month on the tenth day, male and female corpses were found buried under the floorboards. Forensic examination revealed that they had been strangled to death, and the hospital owner Zhang Wenhua and his wives Zhang Yao and Liang Meiyu had all fled without a trace. Only the maid, Mrs. Fei Wang, a native of Wuxi, was apprehended by the police. After investigation, she was released by the Special First Court after questioning, as she had no suspicion of joint criminal conduct. The details have been reported in this newspaper many times.

The case is being handled

by Huang Fugen and Cui Chengke, Chinese detectives from the Huishan Police Station. They are sparing no effort in investigating Zhang Wenhua, Liang Meiyu, and others. All places related to Zhang have been thoroughly investigated. Zhang's father, Zhang Jinsheng, was also summoned by the detectives in order to inquire about his son's whereabouts. At that time, because Zhang Jinsheng's whereabouts were unknown, it was impossible to summon him. Until the afternoon before yesterday, Zhang Jinsheng suddenly arrived at the Huishan Police Station accompanied by two lawyers, Fan Gang and Yu Enliang. According to him, he is from Chuansha, 61 years old, and currently resides at 7 Cihou Nanli, Fuxu Road. His son Zhang Wenhua is 27 years old, studied at McLellan High School, and then worked as a nurse at Shilong Hospital for three years. He is not actually a doctor, and he does not know his whereabouts. He is currently doing his best to investigate so that he can be brought to justice to avoid implicating the innocent. After interrogation by the detectives, it was determined that Zhang Jinsheng was not involved and he was allowed to leave. Then, at 11:30 AM the day before yesterday, the Huishan Police Station suddenly received a notification from the Motor Vehicle Office of the French Concession Police that a local man named Chen Pengfei (23 years old) was currently at the office to obtain a

driver's license.

The person was related to the double corpse case at the Hongkou Hospital. Huang and Cui, two detectives, went there and brought Chen back for investigation. It was learned that Chen was actually the younger brother of the fugitive main suspect, Liang Meiyu. Through Liang's introduction, he started working as a driver for Zhang Wenhua on August 29. The car Zhang drove had license plate number 7203. In addition to the Hongkou Women's Hospital, Zhang also had a clinic at 370 Minguo Road. Zhang went to

both places every day,

and Chen drove him. On September 2, Chen and Zhang drove out of the clinic on Minguo Road, intending to donate and obtain a permit at the French Police Motor Vehicle Office. Since then, Zhang has been using a rickshaw for transportation. According to Chen, on September 1, he saw Zhang Wenhua, Zhang Yao, and Liang Meiyu

together in the consulting room

At that time, there was also a woman about 25 years old sleeping on the bed, with a pale complexion and no blood color. The hair was permed, and the height was five feet four inches, and she seemed to be seriously ill. A man about 30 years old was sitting next to the bed, reading a newspaper, wearing white clothes and pants. He was in extremely good shape. According to the police's judgment, these

two people

may be the corpses that were found. Chen initially lived at 49 Wan, Disui Road, and has now moved to 704 Renzhi Lane, North Sichuan Road. However, he insisted that he did not know the whereabouts of Zhang, Liang, and others. Yesterday morning, the police sent Chen to the Third Criminal Court of the Special First Court. The police lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, explained the circumstances of Chen's arrest, stating that his account was incomplete and untruthful and needed to be thoroughly investigated. Therefore, he requested permission to detain him for a week. After Judge Xiao Xiefen briefly questioned Chen, he ordered that he be detained for a week for further questioning.

Submitted Evidence,

stating that Sun was neither an assistant manager nor a shareholder of the bank. However, the plaintiff's attorney Wu Peng still insisted that Sun was indeed an assistant manager and considered a shareholder, having paid 3,000 yuan of shares. Because the stock was not issued at that time, the money was temporarily treated as a deposit. Huang Yun, a woman who used to answer the phone at the American Chinese Company, testified that she had heard colleagues say that Sun was also a shareholder. Judge Huang adjourned the trial until another date because it was late.

Haili Carries Strange Passengers, Transports Bomb Casings; Four Baskets Filled and Placed in the Cabin; Takes Advantage of Inattention to Go Ashore Again 118

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haili ship, this time returning to Shanghai from Guangzhou, Hong Kong, and Shantou, stopped at Shantou on the afternoon of the 23rd as usual for passengers and cargo to disembark and embark. At that time, two passengers boarded the ship from Shantou, one named Su Yixin and the other named Liu Kechun, claiming to be going to Shanghai. They purchased two seats in the special third-class cabin, and the ship issued two tickets numbered 3388 and 3389. When the two boarded the ship, they carried four large bamboo baskets, which seemed quite heavy. According to Su and Liu, someone would come to take these four bamboo baskets away soon, and they would not be taken to Shanghai, so they were temporarily placed in the cabin. When the two boarded the ship, there were many people picking up and dropping off passengers, and the ship did not have time to pay attention to and inspect the items in the four baskets. When the ship was about to sail, the chief steward Zhuo Zhensheng went to the cabin to check and saw that the four bamboo baskets were still in the cabin. He urgently searched for the two passengers to have them moved away, but the two passengers were nowhere to be found. It was expected that they had taken advantage of the inattention and secretly gone ashore. Zhuo opened the four baskets and found them filled with bomb casings, in large numbers, but without any explosives. Zhuo discussed it with the shipowner and agreed to temporarily hand over the four baskets of bomb casings to the Shantou Bureau and report it by telegram. The Haili ship is still on its way, and the Bureau has decided to thoroughly investigate the matter of the strange passengers transporting bomb casings to clarify the truth.

The two girls, one eighteen and one in their early twenties, are both unmarried. They came to Shanghai this time for the

Sole Purpose.

The reason is that both of them are pregnant and have been for four months. They came to Shanghai specifically to seek medical abortion and to engage in prostitution. However, I feel that abortion is inhumane and dangerous, so I am unwilling to participate in this discussion. However, I regret that the two girls are very determined and fear that they will insist on doing so," etc. When the reporter heard what the young man said, he couldn't help but

be surprised and immediately returned to his residence, and instructed the young man to call the two girls over. After briefly inquiring about their names, one of the girls had received considerable education, and after the reporter persuaded them, and showed them the news previously published in this newspaper about the female worker Wan Lai from Anhui in the Tongxing Yarn Factory on Macao Road who tragically died from abortion due to an impending marriage, one of the girls burst into tears and sobbed for a long time before answering,

"People are not plants,

how can they be without feelings? Even though people are extremely poor, who doesn't cherish their life? Although we (the girl claimed) are weak women from the countryside, we have received considerable education. In recent years, the countryside has gone bankrupt, and we have had no choice but to engage in illicit relations for the sake of livelihood, which is what is called rural prostitutes. But heaven does not pity people, and unfortunately, we have conceived. It has been over four months now. During this early pregnancy, prostitution can still barely be maintained, but after this,

the belly will grow

and it will not be possible to continue. If we wait for it to be formally produced, it will take half a year, and postpartum recuperation will take at least two months. May I ask how will the livelihood problem be solved during this long period of eight months? Therefore, we have been thinking day and night that it is better to take a temporary risk than to wait for formal production and become starving corpses. Our environment is like this, sir (referring to the reporter),

what do you think?"

After the reporter heard this, he was sad for a long time. After repeated consultations, there were three friends present who all expressed their willingness to provide financial assistance, until the two girls were sent to the hospital for delivery and discharged from the hospital. All expenses were fully responsible by the reporter and friends. At this point, the two girls expressed their approval. Recently, according to the two girls, in recent years, there have been many people from Pinghu alone who have come to Shanghai specifically for abortion, and those who have sacrificed their lives because of this are countless.

Traffic Road Fuxing Glass Factory Fire Kills and Injures Two Workers; Explosion Due to Adding Oil to Polishing Machine; Dong Xiaosan Dies, Liu Henglu Injured 121

At about 11:40 yesterday morning, at No. 17, Lane 46, East Traffic Road, Zhabei, the Fuxing Glass Factory suddenly exploded due to adding oil to the polishing machine. With a loud bang, flames shot out and a fire broke out. Worker Dong Xiaosan, a native of Yancheng, 18 years old, was burned to death in the fire. Another worker, Liu Henglu, a native of Yancheng, 18 years old, was severely burned and sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The Hujia Muqiao Hongzhen Fire Brigade, according to the police, drove the pump belt car to the scene and tried their best to put out the fire. The fire was extinguished at 12:45 pm, and four factory buildings were burned down. The factory owner, Ye Guchan, has been detained and sent to the General Bureau for questioning. The body of Dong Xiaosan was inspected by Prosecutor Xu Zenghui from the local court at about 4 pm and ordered to be coffined.

Goods Shipped from Shanghai to Jiangxi to Be Transported by Original Train Across the River 122

Since the Nanchang Station of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway opened to traffic in January this year, goods shipped from Shanghai to Jiangxi and transported by rail have been extremely crowded. However, because the Qiantang River Bridge has not yet been completed, it cannot be directly reached by the original train. The goods must be unloaded from the ship at the Zhakou, transported across the river by barge, and then loaded onto the train. The repeated loading and unloading takes a lot of time. The Jinghu, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, and the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway authorities have specially prepared a ferry to facilitate the transportation of goods and develop combined transportation, which can directly load the original train across the river, which is very fast, without unloading the goods from the ship. It is also stipulated that goods shipped from Shanghai to Nanchang must arrive within three days, which is more than twice as fast as shipping by boat. In the future, freight transportation between Shanghai and Jiangxi will inevitably become more developed. It is reported that the ferry has now been completed and will begin to be used on October 1. Shanghai-Jiangxi cargo merchants will feel endless convenience.

The Jianghai Customs notified various shipping companies yesterday, saying that according to the report of the Customs patrol ship Huaxing, a large wooden ship that had already sunk, 70 feet long, was found in the sea area northeast of Yu Mountain, at 122 degrees 43 minutes east longitude and 32 degrees 12 minutes north latitude. It drifts erratically and hinders the navigation of coastal ships. Please inform the captains of each ship to pay extra attention when passing through this sea area to avoid danger.

Three Bandits Convicted in the Kidnapping of Xue Jiasheng Case; Another Case Discovered Due to Inspection of Handguns; Five People Handed Over to the Public Concession for Trial 125

Xue Jiasheng, the son of the late paint tycoon Xue Baorun, was kidnapped by bandits who broke into his residence at around 4 pm on August 1 while he was taking a nap in his residence. The bandits demanded a huge ransom for his release. On the 14th of the same month, Inspector General Jin Jiulin and Qian Chenglong of the Special Agency of the French Police, detectives Zhou Bingcheng and Zhou Buguang, led detectives on duty to investigate and solve the case. The kidnapped person was found safely in the agency at No. 222 Pushi Road because the kidnappers fled upon hearing the news. At the same time, the detectives successively arrested the kidnappers Chen Jintang (40 years old, Anhui native), Bu Mingqing (42 years old, Xuzhou native), Sun Yanan (38 years old, Yancheng native), Pu Yaozhang (55 years old, Yangzhou native), and Wu Genyou (39 years old, Ningbo native) at No. 72 Delong Village, Julai Road, and seized Mauser pistols, Browning pistols, and bullets. They were sent to the Second Special Court. The police lawyer filed a public prosecution in accordance with the law. After repeated trials by the Criminal Judge Wang Gangxu, the judgment was scheduled. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday, when the judgment was due, at 2 pm, Judge Wang and Clerk Gao Yan visited the Criminal Court and ordered the five defendants to be brought to the case. After briefly questioning their ages and origins, the judgment was announced. Chen Jintang was sentenced to 15 years of imprisonment and 10 years of deprivation of civil rights for jointly intending to extort a ransom and kidnap people. Bu Mingqing (same crime) was sentenced to life imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for life. Wu Genyou (same crime) was sentenced to 12 years of imprisonment and 10 years of deprivation of civil rights. The handguns and bullets were confiscated. Sun Yanan and Pu Yaozhang were found not guilty. Furthermore, because the Medical Office found that one of the handguns seized in the case was opened in the case of plotting to kidnap Lu Dengyu at the intersection of Carter Road and Aven Avenue in the Public Concession on June 12 this year, the Xinzha Police Station requested the First Special District Court to send a document to the Second Special Court requesting that the five defendants be transferred to the case for investigation and trial. After the Judge of the Civil Court reviewed the official document, he instructed that the five defendants be handed over to the officers to take them away for trial.

Sues for Confirmation of Guardianship After Death of Brother and Sister-in-Law; Zhuang Zezhong et al. v. Feng Peigeng et al. Concluded Debate Yesterday and Scheduled Judgment 130

Zhuang Zezhong and Zhuang Zeren, local residents who currently reside at No. 25, Lane 288, Beck Road in the Public Concession and work as senior officials in the Jianghai Customs, hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the Civil Court of the Second Special Court against Feng Dazhang, the father-in-law of their deceased brother Zexin, and Feng Peigeng, Feng Peikun, and Feng Peizhi, the sisters of their deceased sister-in-law, seeking confirmation of guardianship rights. The complaint stated that the plaintiff's deceased brother Zhuang Zexin had been working in the customs service and married the defendant Feng Dazhang's youngest daughter Peiyu, with whom he had an eldest daughter, Huizhi (nine years old this year). His younger brother Zexin died unexpectedly on April 2, 1934 (drowned in the river). His sister-in-law Peiyu raised the orphaned son and daughter. At that time, Zexin received several thousand in customs pensions after his death, and private savings of about ten thousand yuan, all of which were kept by his sister-in-law. Since Zexin's death, his sister-in-law has been depressed all day long, and died in the hospital on July 28 last year. All of Peiyu's inheritance was in the hands of the defendants. After Peiyu's death, she left behind a son and a daughter, who were initially raised by the plaintiffs. However, the defendants, fearing that they would demand Peiyu's inheritance, took Huizhi and Zhengda away under the pretext of raising their nephews and nieces at the plaintiffs' place. The plaintiffs stated that the Zhuang family's flesh and blood could not be raised by others for a long time, so they filed a lawsuit requesting a judgment confirming their guardianship rights. Yesterday morning, the court, based on the complaint, summoned the defendants to the Civil Court 7, presided over by Judge Ma Yishu. The defendants hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to defend on their behalf, requesting that the plaintiffs' lawsuit be dismissed. After the court questioned both parties in detail, it ordered the debate to begin and announced its conclusion, scheduling the judgment for the 29th of this month.

County Administration - General Inspection of Opium 136

In Shanghai County, it has been more than half a year since the implementation of the general inspection of opium in various districts. However, after County Chief Li Zhifu took office, he paid considerable attention to the prohibition policy. Considering that prolonged periods lead to complacency, and fearing that public officials in various districts might become negligent, he specifically instructed a general inspection to be completed by the end of this month. It is understood that all officials in the political and police circles of each district made a solemn pledge to eradicate opium, and their responsibilities are crucial. Therefore, after receiving the order, the heads of each district and township, along with the heads of the public security bureaus and stations, have been visiting opium dens and selling and smoking locations to investigate private sales and smoking. They are also using the baojia system to search house by house for private smokers and repeat offenders, requiring the heads of the jia to provide proof. After the deadline, the county government will send personnel to conduct secret investigations at any time.

Common Sense for Treating Lung Disease 148

— Dr. Shen Zhaoquan

—Do Not Blindly Believe in the Delusion of Chemical Drugs to Kill Bacteria—

The lung disease medicines sold on the market today are numerous and countless. Their exaggerated claims of efficacy are all illusions after clinical trials, exposing their complete ineffectiveness. However, many lung disease patients are deceived by them, leading to delays in proper treatment and putting themselves in an incurable situation.

The pathogen of pulmonary tuberculosis is the tubercle bacillus. Those with a little scientific knowledge generally know this. This bacterium has extremely strong resistance, and it is not easy to eradicate with any drug. Although the progress of modern medicine is rapid, there is still no specific drug that can directly kill the tubercle bacillus. Our principle of treating tuberculosis is to increase the body's resistance and indirectly cure the disease, not to directly kill the bacteria.

Although there are many drugs that can directly kill tubercle bacilli in test tubes in chemical laboratories, they all have strong toxicity. If they are used in the human body, the human body will inevitably suffer great damage before the tubercle bacilli are killed. Moreover, drugs, whether taken internally or injected, must pass through blood vessels and circulate throughout the body to the lesion to exert their effect. However, the tuberculosis lesion is in a corner of the lung tissue and has no blood vessels. Even if there is a safe bactericidal drug, its efficacy cannot be manifested. In other words, the place where the pathogens multiply cannot be reached by the drug. Therefore, the unreliability of the effect of such chemical drugs on tubercle bacilli in the body is evident.

Chronic diseases invading the prostate often cause such prostatic fluid leakage and spermatorrhea.

Next World Games Winter Sports Location Issue To Be Decided Next June 160

(Guomin Haitong News Agency) Lausanne, September 23. Although the 12th Olympic Games in 1940 will be held in Tokyo, the 5th Olympic Winter Games may not be held in Japan. Therefore, the location issue has not yet been decided.

Olympic International Committee Secretary Pataz told reporters today that a country that organizes the Summer Games has the right of first refusal to organize the other games if its position permits. Japan has not formally announced that it will give up this right. It is a candidate for the 1940 Olympic Winter Games. In addition, there are Canada, St. Moritz, and Oslo. The location issue will be decided in Warsaw in the second week of June 1937. However, the reception committee will meet in Lausanne before that date.

Foreign Nationals in Shanghai Initiate Car and Motorcycle Races Next Month on the 18th at the Yinxiang Port Racecourse There will also be Men's and Women's Cycling Races 161

German national Ebbert and American national Klenhsing Lee, who reside in Shanghai, plan to set up a Far East Car and Motorcycle Racing Association in Shanghai. The office is located at Room 200 of the Citibank Building, 45 Jiujiang Road. They will hold car and motorcycle races on the 18th of next month at the Yangshupu Yinxiang Port Racecourse. Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, the association specially invited Chinese and foreign reporters from Shanghai to a tea party at the Lido Garden on Matt Hurst Road. The founder of the association, Klen, reported on the purpose of holding the competition, which is to encourage the cultivation of physique, intelligence, courage, and skill. Although this type of sport is common in Europe and America, it is still a pioneering effort to hold it in China. Therefore, the field equipment is not very comprehensive. The cars used in the competition are also not limited to cars specifically designed for competition, in order to show universality. Fortunately, they were able to obtain the approval of the municipal government and were able to hold the event at the Yangshupu Yinxiang Port Racecourse, which is very grateful. At the same time, they plan to set up a car exhibition at the venue to collect all kinds of cars and display them at the venue to enhance the grand occasion. As for the competition schedule, it is currently set as three car races, three motorcycle races, two men's cycling races, and one women's cycling race. The qualifications for competitors are limited to amateurs. Professional athletes will be excluded. There is no limit to nationality. Chinese and foreign men and women can join as competitors. However, the cars must be self-provided. After the association sends personnel to inspect the equipment, they can participate. The physical fitness must also be checked to determine acceptance. The prizes will be donated by all walks of life and are being contacted by all parties. In order to limit the crowding of the audience, seats will be set up in the racecourse and admission tickets will be charged. The ticket prices are set at four types: five yuan, three yuan, one yuan, and five cents. 15% of the ticket income will be used as the China Aviation Construction Association's funds or to purchase airplanes to celebrate Jiang's birthday. Competitors can contact the association's office from next week to register. This competition is still a pioneering effort in China and is expected to be warmly welcomed by Chinese and foreign people at that time.

Education News

Japan's Compulsory Education Expenses Local Expenses Borne by the State Currently Set at 175 Million Yuan 164

(Tokyo Communication) China has been promoting compulsory education for the past year, and has made considerable progress. Japan is also implementing compulsory education at the same time. Japan takes primary schools as compulsory education, which is the same meaning as China taking short-term primary schools as compulsory education. Regarding the issue of Japan's education funding, it has now been resolved. The expenses that were previously borne by the city, town, and village residents, totaling 136 million yuan, have now been completely abolished and will be borne by the state. The majority of this is for compulsory education and primary school teachers' salaries. The national compulsory education and primary school education expenses in Japan are 175 million yuan, which are now also completely borne by the state. In the future, the Ministry of Education (equivalent to China's Ministry of Education) will have greater responsibilities and greater authority to guide compulsory education. China's compulsory education funding stipulated last year that the local government would pay half and the central government would subsidize the other half. Those who are concerned about this education can refer to Japan's compulsory funding. (Qin)

Recent Five-Year Education Expenditure in Anhui Province: Provincial and County Funds Increasing Year by Year 165

Anhui Province's education expenditure for the recent five years is calculated as follows: In the 20th year, provincial funds amounted to 2,758,580 yuan, county funds amounted to 2,489,779 yuan, totaling 5,248,359 yuan. In the 21st year, provincial funds amounted to 2,636,581 yuan, county funds amounted to 2,748,216 yuan, totaling 5,384,797 yuan. In the 22nd year, provincial funds amounted to 2,699,515 yuan, county funds amounted to 2,890,489 yuan, totaling 5,590,024 yuan. In the 23rd year, provincial funds amounted to 2,755,065 yuan, county funds amounted to 2,427,071 yuan, totaling 5,182,136 yuan. In the 24th year, provincial funds amounted to 2,918,933 yuan, county funds amounted to 2,355,870 yuan, totaling 5,274,803 yuan. Taking the 24th year as an example,

The provincial funds of 2,918,933 yuan were allocated as follows: 112,773 yuan for educational administration, 544,189 yuan for higher education, 1,458,906 yuan for secondary education, 220,708 yuan for primary education, 230,000 yuan for compulsory education, 136,122 yuan for social education, and 6,235 yuan for other education. The total is 2,918,933 yuan. Further analysis:

In higher education, the recurring expenses of Anhui University amounted to 315,149 yuan, public funds for students studying abroad amounted to 118,088 yuan, scholarships for students studying abroad amounted to 91,152 yuan, and scholarships for domestic university students amounted to 19,800 yuan, totaling 544,189 yuan.

In secondary education, middle school education amounted to 609,907 yuan, accounting for 41.98%, and vocational education amounted to 440,849 yuan, accounting for 30.22%, totaling 1,458,906 yuan.

In primary education, the recurring expenses of normal schools and middle school affiliated primary schools amounted to 145,776 yuan, provincial capital primary schools amounted to 160,176 yuan, subsidies and other items amounted to 24,756 yuan, totaling 330,708 yuan. In compulsory education, the source of funds was the national treasury (20,000 yuan), the Gengzi Indemnity (10,000 yuan), the provincial treasury (80,000 yuan), the surplus from previous years' study abroad expenses (90,000 yuan), and the county local reserve fund (30,000 yuan), totaling 230,000 yuan. These funds were allocated to short-term primary schools (180,000 yuan), short-term primary school classes (16,000 yuan), the two-part system (11,500 yuan), compulsory private schools (27,500 yuan), textbook compilation (20,000 yuan), itinerant teaching (10,000 yuan), teacher training (15,000 yuan), administrative guidance (20,000 yuan), and special subsidies to various counties (10,000 yuan), totaling 330,000 yuan. Taking the 24th year as an example,

The county funds of 2,355,870 yuan came from the 61 counties in Anhui, including over 990,000 yuan from surcharges on land tax, over 270,000 yuan from surcharges on deed tax, over 40,000 yuan from surcharges on broker's fees, over 150,000 yuan from surcharges on livestock slaughter tax, over 560,000 yuan from school property rental income, and over 350,000 yuan from other and temporary income. These over 2,350,000 yuan were allocated by the education bureaus of each county for the education expenses of all levels in their respective counties.

Jiangsu Province Reorganizes School Property in Various Counties 167

The educational land property in various counties of Jiangsu Province ranges from several thousand mu in a small county to tens of thousands of mu in a large county, and even hundreds of thousands of mu in some cases, totaling a considerable amount. In the past, due to improper management, numerous abuses arose. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, in view of this, first formulated measures to centralize the educational property and transfer it to the management of the Education Bureau, in order to unify authority and prevent malpractices. However, as many school lands in various counties had been encroached upon, concealed, or abandoned for many years, resulting in loss and difficulty in investigation, it also revised measures for clearing school lands and rectifying school rents (including methods for surveying, measuring, mapping, etc.). Furthermore, supplementary methods for clearing school lands and rectifying school rents were drafted and designated as one of the central tasks when the administrative guidelines for the 24th year were issued to various counties. Simultaneously, special commissioners for inspecting school property were dispatched to various counties to conduct on-site inspections and formulate appropriate rectification plans based on the previous abuses of school property in each county, ordering guidance and implementation. After repeated urging and rectification, the school property in various counties has achieved significant results, which can be summarized as follows: (1) Gaoyou, Shiying, Yancheng, Dangshan, and Si County have used the revenue from rectification to repurchase school lands that had been mortgaged. (2) After rectification, Yancheng increased its rental income by approximately 10,000 yuan in the 24th year. (3) The disputes over school property in Funing were significant, but after rectification, it has become quite stable. (4) Gaoyou increased its school land by over 300 mu (purchased with compensation from the former Education Bureau Chief, Qiu). (5) After rectification in Liyang, the opening of the Sanda Polder can increase revenue by tens of thousands of yuan annually. (6) After rectification in Guanyun, all school property in the city and townships has been taken over by the Bureau, and the phenomenon of manipulation and disputes has been eliminated. (7) Huaian has just begun rectification, and it is estimated that the school rent revenue for the 25th year will increase by 10,000 yuan compared to the previous year. (8) Tongshan and Pei County have completed rectification, but unfortunately suffered from the Yellow River flood, and rent payments could not be collected in full. However, the abuses have been eliminated. (9) Other counties, such as Yangzhou and Lianshui, have also implemented surveys of school property and submitted maps for record. At a time when national compulsory education is being implemented, the central government deeply understands the difficulties of the people and is raising substantial funds for subsidies. Local governments should also find ways to reorganize the sources of education funding in order to discuss major plans and achieve early success. However, considering the current social and economic situation, excessive and miscellaneous taxes should be abolished, and the people's capacity to bear burdens should not be exceeded. The current plan is to reorganize the school property allocated to education expenses in various counties, which can provide some support. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has instructed the heads of various county bureaus to work together to achieve the goal of thorough reorganization.

Securities: People Panic, Public Debt Plummets Suddenly, Big Investors Sell Off Heavily, Plummeting by 1.5 Yuan, Today Trading for One Month of October 178

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange suddenly experienced drastic changes in the market, with a very fierce drop. The sudden incident in Hongkou happened on the last day of September futures, and the market was squeezed, resulting in extreme intensity. In addition, the outflow of spot goods and market rumors that someone in the financial world sold off made people feel even more panicked. Even the numbers that had always been very stable sold off in large quantities at this point, such as 11, 43, and 54. Either bulls were coming out of their cages, or spot goods were flowing out. The dull situation turned into an extremely active market. It is difficult to predict how the future will evolve. Today, only one month of October futures will be traded, and the fluctuations in the market should be slightly reduced. According to the dealers, the morning opening for this month's E bond fell slightly, with some bears offsetting, but the distant contracts could not support it and quickly fell by a small 0.7 yuan. After that, the fall intensified. The wind and waves of selling by numbers 11, 43, and 54 surged. The B bond fell by 0.95 yuan, the most, a rare market scene in recent times. The E bond broke through the 60-yuan mark. The second round of short covering was even worse, falling another 0.5-0.6 yuan. The C bond also broke through the 60-yuan mark. Rumors spread in the market. The afternoon opening for the national bond D fell sharply by 0.95 yuan, almost breaking through the 60-yuan mark. After entering, number 43 slightly covered shorts, and types A and B were slightly better by 0.2-0.3 yuan. The closing was suddenly distorted due to the enthusiastic buying by numbers 32, 33, and 4 of the Unified E and D bonds, and the short covering trend rose, rebounding by 0.3-0.4 yuan. The recent rise in the D bond was good by 0.95 yuan. However, after the Unified C, numbers 54 and 11 continued to sell off in large amounts, and the market turned weak again. Rumors resurfaced, and people became even more panicked. Unified B and A fell by another 0.25 to 0.6 yuan. As a result of the closing, the previous results plummeted by 0.75 to 1.5 yuan. 96 also fell slightly by 0.4 yuan. The total number of transactions was 17.68 million yuan. A comparison of the highs and lows of the price increases and decreases is listed in the table on the left (unit: yuan, transaction unit: 100 yuan).

Sanyang Maru

Gauze Flowers: Spot Sales Active, Gauze Market's Decline Slows, Many Eager to Buy on Dips 180

The gauze market is calm, but the trend is good, and sentiment is unusually enthusiastic, with most people bullish. This is due to the lively spot gauze sales, the gradual movement of gauze from warehouses, and the market's adoption of a "buy on dips" strategy for cotton yarn. However, the overseas gauze flower market situation is remarkably dull. It is said that there is some negative sentiment within, tending towards selling.

Standard Gauze Opens with a Dip 181

At the opening of the standard gauze market this morning, prices for all months showed a decline. Due to [unspecified] events, sentiment was poor, and floating accounts sold off, weakening momentum. Prices fell by five, six, or seven jiao for near-term months and one yuan for distant months. After the second session, it was heard that spot gauze sales remained strong, buying interest revived, and market prices rebounded. It was observed that the willingness to sell was strong from Xincheng [Trustworthy], Deda [Great Virtue], Hexing [Harmonious Prosperity], Gengfeng [Perpetual Abundance], and Fukang [Blessing and Health], while Yuda [Great Abundance] also covered short positions significantly. Xingchang [Prosperous Chang], Huamao [Magnificent China], and Xiacheng [Harmonious Achievement] all bought in. By the close, the market situation was ordinary. As a result, the closing prices for each month of standard gauze were down three, four, or six jiao compared to the previous month's closing prices. In the afternoon session, the market appeared flat, with distant contracts weaker. After the second session, it was heard that spot gauze business still involved over 2,000 bales, and sentiment revived.
