Not Nostalgia 196

— Zigang

It's evening, and there's still not a bit of wind. Stepping out of the printing house, the scorching steam still rushes at my nose. There are particularly many cars out for a spin in the evening. The bright Shell and Socony signs squint dreamily. I take a breath: the ink smell from the typesetting room has been replaced by the even more unpleasant gasoline.

I hurry back along the sidewalk, with not a trace of imagination in my head. A day's work has made me forget everything, leaving only this bit of hunger, which constantly suggests, protesting to me.

Under a street lamp, I received a heavy blow on my shoulder.

"Hey, it's you! How many years has it been, how many years—" The speaker was clearly surrounded by a sudden surge of excitement, a bit breathless. The nose, thin and particularly tall for a middle-aged man, was the clearest marker: wasn't that my distant uncle who was in the silk business?

"Big Nose, are you here to sell goods again?" I shook his thin, blue-veined hand. However, because they were hidden in long sleeves all year round, they were white and皙. I didn't have time to see if the wedding ring from seven years ago still had its former charm on that white hand.

He wasn't surprised at all by the impolite nickname and laughed innocently, but quickly collected himself: "Wild child, what are you running around for all day? Don't you miss home? Now that you're so close, you don't even come back to see, you could at least come visit Uncle Big Nose!"

I turned around and pointed to the place I had just come out of, telling him that it was where I worked.

"Be careful of your lungs!" He suddenly warned me with concern. He still remembered my congenital deficiency.

I didn't answer him for a moment, just kept walking with him towards my home. When we reached a car dealership on the corner, Big Nose's eyes flashed, and he casually read the signs on the large glass window.

"1936, hmm, a very difficult year! So many bizarre things have come out:" He seemed to have a flash of inspiration, touching on the depression in his heart, and sighed:

"Do you know? Our landlord, Master Han the Fourth, hanged himself! That opium addict, because of two years of empty fields, couldn't be a small landlord anymore. He started selling the house, and last year the county chased him to pay taxes. He ran and ran, avoiding the wind. But what about food? There was even still black rice to eat! That middle-aged fellow just last month——."

"Damn it all! These obstacles of the vigorous, the middle-aged, the old, their fates are all the same, sooner or later you'll see! Hey, didn't Master Han the Fourth's young wife take out a teaching diploma from her dowry chest to become a primary school teacher?" I grabbed this bit of history from my vague memories.

Big Nose patted my shoulder: "Good girl, it's wrong to say you have no conscience towards your hometown, you remember everything. Hmm, that young lady who's a teacher? A primary school teacher with twenty yuan a month can't do much to support Master Han the Fourth. That woman has a lot of ideas, she's also smart. She taught for half a year with a lot of energy, and in the end she took all three children away, telling the opium addict: 'I'm taking the children, you take care of yourself!' You see, that was a clean break, without money, the opium addict couldn't throw his weight around……"

We stepped over the piles of people on the sidewalk. People had closed the narrow doors of their homes and run to the street to cool off. The homeless men and children found dark corners to lie down and rest, often getting hit with a stick or a shoe in their dreams.

"These days!" Big Nose looked at the piles of people with worry, as if afraid that one day this misfortune, this suffering, would weigh on him. He had a slight cold premonition, and the middle-aged man's gloom deepened day by day. He had heard the news of losses at their shop, and at the end of the year there was a shortage of working capital, almost forcing them to close.

"Think about who makes us live these days! Uncle, do you know about the roar of the peasants in the suburbs of our hometown recently? In the future——" I can't forget the recent historical materials of my hometown, which are the only things that excite me. The feeders of the fat pigs that have been buried underground for many years are also rising up.

A burst of childish enthusiasm made me look at the dark sky. It will be bright tomorrow, won't it? So I puffed out my chest.

"That, it's too wild, but, it's also a reason, although a little sacrifice is needed…… The hometown has also changed, even in the teahouse, the loud laughter has been overwhelmed by some poor worries, everyone sighs in the manner of being drunk about the sweeping star that has overwhelmed paradise, counting down the helplessness of life, not many people have the spare money and leisure to call out to a ballad seller, or eat some eel noodles or shrimp dumplings. There are also fewer people organizing gambling games here: gambling and gambling is debt, no fun. It's really time to see this declining small town!"

I slowed down a little, ignoring his advice, and another thought came up:

"How many, cousins and younger siblings do I have? Big Nose!"

His sunken eyes moved: "Silly ghost, you've even forgotten this, what thin affection! But who's to blame? Your Big Nose aunt is too good at having children. By this winter, Little Five will be born soon. Our shop is worse every year, and at the end of the year there's not much bonus, the boss even wants to close down! He says we're 'eating together,' we can't get any good out of it, and we have to worry, it's also strange, silk at two mao a foot has few buyers, rayon, the immoral stuff, has squeezed the silk factories in our hometown to close their doors, piles of mulberry leaves watch them sprout and leaf on the trees, let them wither and fall to the ground! The clever ones have even dug up the roots!"

He poured out a bellyful of grievances as if he was letting out air: "Your aunt told me not to eat this bowl of rice anymore, to open a small shop happily, but women really don't understand the difficulty. A big shop can't be opened, and a small shop isn't enough to live on. Do you know Zhu Laoer, who went from being an 'artist' (he said it with special emphasis, I know he means the one who used to set the scenery for the civilization troupe) to opening a grocery store? At first he was so impressive, traveling to the docks, speaking official language, but these days he's being squeezed for the rent of the small grocery store, borrowing from everywhere, but the year——" Big Nose faltered for a moment, "Isn't it harder to borrow money than for a rooster to lay an egg?"

"…… But, desperate measures, little by little people will……"

Big Nose immediately took over: "This Zhu Laoer has already jumped over the wall! That day the landlord found the police to force rent, saying he would break the counter if he didn't pay. The nearly fifty-year-old Zhu Laoer really got angry, pointing to his own pasteboard devices (this is an involuntary sideline, he's a scenery-builder!) and thrusting his fist to the police's hat: 'You want it, I'll give you this, I'll send you to the West! I'm telling you: you can't squeeze oil out of a stone!' Hey, my wild child, Zhu Laoer ate a series of slaps, his face flushed, grabbed a bench and……

(Zhu Laoer is a prominent figure on this street, he's traveled to the docks, been out of the province, how could he stand this!)"

Without him saying it, I had already guessed the result; "There's no telling how many years he'll be sentenced to, it's just that Zhu Laoer's wife is still making trouble with her children at the prison, wanting to serve her time together, she says that outside she has hands that can work but no food to eat, it's better to eat 'gravel rice' together……"

Big Nose's face flushed with excitement, I seemed to see it. The hand he was holding got hotter and hotter, I knew what kind of excitement was leaping in his heart. Finally, he tugged at his silk gown:

"There will be a time, Uncle Big Nose will take off this silk gown, really, do you believe it, wild thing? Really take it off——will you still pay attention to Uncle then?"

I was stunned by his innocent question. I happily said, "Why wouldn't I pay attention? Not only will I pay attention, but I'll also hold Big Nose's hand tightly and walk together, like today." I smiled comfortably.

Big Nose also smiled half-knowingly.

"We're home, are you coming in?" I stopped in front of a noisy alleyway.

"No," he looked at his watch, "it's too late, I was originally looking for a colleague, the store had some debts from when it closed, they called me to handle it. I'll go back tomorrow—"

Under the echo of his well-intentioned "You should come back and take a look too!" I took out the key to open the back door.

A bit of annoyance, a bit of surprise, a bit of disorder mixed in my heart, I was a little dazed, but—

Not nostalgia!

A few stars are twinkling behind the black curtain of the sky.

"Tomorrow will be a clear day," I thought to myself.

Simplicity and Complexity in Characters 197

— Qu Yi

(1)

In order to attract readers, the best way to portray characters in a work is to simplify them.

Simplification means that a hero must be a hero through and through, and a rogue must be a rogue through and through.

But why can such simplified characters attract readers? Perhaps the reason is that our lives are not very complex, and we cannot understand all the actions and thoughts of the complex characters depicted. A typical example is that middle school students generally like to read emotional or sentimental works.

But perhaps there are other reasons.

This fact can be exemplified by the popularity of Jiang Guangchi's novels a few years ago, which specialized in writing about revolutionaries who were revolutionaries through and through. Even now, although this style has changed slightly, when writing about ridiculous characters, they are always depicted with a face smeared with white powder, as if the character has no serious side apart from their ridiculous life; when portraying revolutionaries or patriotic heroes, they always have a cold face, or a sad face, or a flushed face to the end, as if those people live in a vacuum, with no private lives of their own. Works like that are still welcomed to this day.

Of course, our authors also know that the simplification of characters is somewhat unrealistic. Therefore, when portraying characters, they understand the changes in the character's personality. They skillfully match the characters with the environment, turning the character from one extreme to the other, such as turning a non-revolutionary person into a revolutionary in a revolutionary environment, or turning a passive or weak-willed person into an active or strong-willed person under certain circumstances. Thus, the reader is also inspired by the character's transformation and is ultimately captivated by the author.

The truth is that this approach is still another variation of simplification, changing from the simple extreme A to the simple extreme B. It is just a matter of putting two simple characters together. Compared with real characters, the distance is still very far.

The reason for this is that the author has no hands-on experience with life. Without hands-on experience with life, relying only on hearsay or cold observation, the author will never understand life.

However, as an author, one has to pretend to understand life. Thus, clever authors, relying on their so-called correct concepts, prop up the characters with a framework, dress them in clothes, slightly sketch their features, and make them act mechanically. But the so-called action is still in the hands of the surrogate, becoming a puppet show.

This is probably the characteristic of formulaic works! And the formation of formulas is probably due to the author's empty life!

But there are also many authors who have indeed had hands-on experience with life. However, in their writing, there is often the suspicion that the characters are too simplified. Although the characters are simple, they are quite vivid, and not mechanically simple. The reason for this is that the author pays too much attention to the reader's taste, and must find a way to arouse the reader's interest with a certain appearance and certain words and deeds; then, from the real characters they are familiar with, they abstract the components they want that match their theme to construct a kind of theatrical character. This is what makes it a novel after all. However, once it relies on the novel and makes the reader not forget that it is a novel when reading it, then its distance from the reality of reality has already been slightly farther. Here, we do not deny the components extracted from real characters in constructing characters; the problem is that to construct a living character, it is necessary to extract various essential or decisive components from various real characters and combine them to make them typical. Typification is definitely not simplification.

The simplicity of the characters written by some authors is due to their obsession with realism. Those who love to write about real-life characters often get bogged down on the surface of the characters, unable to delve into the inner lives of real-life characters. Sometimes, moreover, the author's degree of love or hate for real-life characters in terms of human affairs is used to give them extreme affirmation or extreme denial. The worst result of this tendency is the use of literary works as personal attacks. The reality of reality is veiled by the author's subjective perspective. The author's baseness is exposed, and the attacked characters are obscured and cannot be seen.

The simplicity of characters created by these two creative methods, although not completely divorced from the reality of reality, cannot show the full picture of real characters. The so-called full picture of real characters is not an accurate record of a certain real character, but refers to the typical transcendence of the character.

(3)

In real-life characters, generally speaking, the hard-working are relatively simple, and the intellectual class is more complex. But this is only a difference in degree. Simplicity will never be simple through and through, as shown in our past revolutionary literary works, like heroes.

When Gorky wrote about his Malva and Chelkash, they seemed to be relatively simple. But they also have their complexities. Malva's love for the father and son is different, and her love for another rogue is even different. The sensations in her heart are complex, although her whole character is strung together with a simple, promiscuous woman's lines. But it is precisely this way of writing that makes Malva alive.

But when he wrote about Klim Samgin, he described them with complex lines, and in the end, he revealed the simplicity of the life of this character from the intellectual class.

In the third part of the novel The Bystander, Gorky similarly portrays Marina, an extremely complex intellectual woman. She sympathizes with the revolution and sometimes even financially supports the revolution, but she actually enters and exits the doors of the aristocracy, advocating for sectarianism and inheriting other people's property, verbally wanting to replace God with the spirit, but in reality only caring about making money, and using various sensual actions to seduce Klim Samgin, who is her lawyer. This person can truly be said to be extremely complex, but in the end, it cannot be denied that she is also simple. In the work and lives of these two people, apart from sitting and talking about everything, and being concerned with material desires, there is never anything else to do. Marina criticizes Klim Samgin, saying:

"You intellectuals are accustomed to using many questions to decorate yourselves and show off to others. You flaunt complexity, as if saying, 'See who is more complex?' And you are just making each other entangled. Because the solution to the problem does not come from reason, but from will... Reason is just helping from the side. Only the will can teach people how to walk freely."

These words are extremely correct. But Marina herself is also extremely mysteriously complex. Here, we only hear the correctness of all Marina's statements, but her actions make people feel mysterious. She advocates sectarianism and opposes Christianity; and she sympathizes with the revolution and provides assistance to revolutionaries. She wants to improve Klim Samgin's spirit, which seems to be dominated by laziness, and finally uses the fiery belief—spiritual belief—to seduce him, but instead scares him away, and he finally leaves Marina. This is truly an extremely complex, detailed depiction, and readers who do not have patience will find it difficult to finish the whole story.

The characters dealt with in Chinese works can be said to be mostly intellectuals. But the intellectuals we see in the works are so simple that they only make people love or hate; perhaps Chinese intellectuals are relatively simple. But they also have their sorrows and joys, anger and calmness, timidity and determination, their conscience towards the group and private desires, and their sense of justice and ideas of rights—why does no one express these mutually contradictory and conflicting personalities? The characters in our writers' works really demand too much simplification.

But we are still waiting. Waiting for the appearance of complex characters who depict the complexity of an era. Although this is relatively unpopular with readers, the complex era will advance the reader's understanding!

Ah Hua's Death 198

— Lin Shi

It was actually this spring, but she—Ah Hua—her impression on me has burned into my heart, thinking about it now, it is as clear as if it happened this morning.

The matter is like this: My landlord, Mrs. Lü, in order to squeeze two pounds of beef juice for her two chubby sons every day, had a lot of beef residue left over that had no taste at all. It would be a pity to just throw it in the trash can, and it wouldn't be appropriate to give it to beggars, so she asked her son-in-law—the fourth aunt's husband—for a female cat. Naturally, on the one hand, it was to catch mice, and on the other hand, it was simply to use it as a digestion machine for the beef residue. This finally solved the serious problem that Mrs. Lü had been thinking about for a long time. Mrs. Lü gave this cat a very appropriate name: Ah Hua, because its whole body was a jumble of yellow, white, and black.

I didn't like Ah Hua very much, it wasn't all white, nor all black, which didn't fit my prejudice about cats. Needless to say, this had nothing to do with it, it wasn't mine, I didn't have the responsibility to raise it, only Mrs. Lü never forgot to teach the maid to give it beef residue to eat every day. Before long, it became fat.

Spring quietly came to the world and quietly left. At that time, Ah Hua had been calling in front and behind the house for several nights, but later it stopped calling. But I unintentionally discovered that Ah Hua was even fatter and its belly was getting bigger, I knew it was about to become a mother. At the same time, I also found a male cat following it around, which made me curious. I asked my wife, and she told me that it was Ah Hua's husband, who had been recruited a month ago. Oh! I laughed in realization, my wife also laughed, but Mrs. Lü's consideration was very different from ours. She deeply hated this foreign cat, which had to share half of Ah Hua's beef residue, and felt it was too inappropriate, so she often chased the male cat with a wooden stick, drove it out of the door, and didn't allow it to come in again. But after a while, Ah Hua and it could be found hiding under the kitchen table, meowing. It was really too easy for it to sneak in through the window or under the iron door.

One night, it was during the Qingming Festival, and the drizzle outside the window was very bleak. Everyone in the house was asleep, only I was still bent over my desk, groping in the light of an old lamp. A cat was calling, its intermittent cries filling the front and back, up and down, terribly. I could tell that it was Ah Hua, its voice was too familiar to me. But why was it crying? Who had hurt it? It made me think of a wife who had lost her husband, a mother who had lost her son, this tragic cry of the world, piercing my still heart, and at the same time making me unbearable. I went to chase and beat Ah Hua in anger, regardless of whether this action was cruel; but when I got close to it, it quickly ran away. However, it was still meowing, obviously my threat could not stop its sorrow. In this way, I was disturbed by it and could not get a moment of peace of mind, so I had to stop my work and angrily wake up my wife who had already fallen asleep. My wife told me that Mrs. Lü had told the coachman, Ah Er, to drive the male cat several streets away, so that it wouldn't recognize its way back to guard its wife who was about to give birth, which was why Ah Hua was crying; so my heart turned cold.

Ah Hua cried all night, and cried again the next day, but its husband didn't hear its voice, and from then on it lived alone for a long time, until it gave birth.

Ah Hua gave birth to two kittens, I don't remember exactly when, but according to my wife, one of them was born lame, and I didn't care much about it. As for why she told me this, there was also a reason: it turned out that Ah Hua had jumped onto my family's cupboard and smashed all the bowls inside, making my wife so angry that her face turned pale. I said:

"Ah Hua must be hungry, so it stole to eat."

"That's right," my wife replied, "Mrs. Lü's children don't eat beef juice anymore, and Ah Hua doesn't have beef residue to eat, and they don't even give it enough to eat with stinky fish and rice, and it has to feed the kittens with milk, how can it not be greedy?"

"Are the kittens fun? Are they all white?"

"Fun? One of them was born lame and can't even walk."

I don't know if Mrs. Lü hated it because it gave birth to a lame son? Or was there another reason? One night I found Ah Hua catching goldfish in the fish tank in front of my window to eat, I proved that it was really starving. Sure enough, the next day Mrs. Lü found that the fish tank was missing a "dragon seed" and gave Ah Hua a good beating.

It is of course an extremely ordinary thing for a cat to be beaten for stealing food, but sometimes it can make you realize the sadness of life from an animal. For its own hunger, and for the hunger of its children, is it the greatest sin to be forced to steal? Because of this, I was also melancholy for a while, but before long I forgot about it again.

"Dad, come and see, little Ah Mi is jumping in the kitchen!"

One morning, my four-year-old child happily told me this, and immediately dragged me to the kitchen. Sure enough, one of the two kittens was clumsily snatching the paper ball tied with a thread in the maid's hand, Ah Hua was watching from the side, and the other lame one was not moving at all, only occasionally making a weak cry. Ah Hua saw the child's jumping and naturally had infinite joy, but when the lame one could not move, it just stared at it with sadness. It used its front paw to nudge it, meaning to tell it to stand up, and then jumped around itself to teach it, but the lame child just meowed and didn't move at all. Once, twice, three times, Ah Hua was exhausted and had to sit aside, watching it motionless, and even the jumping of the other child didn't arouse its interest. After a while, it lowered its tail and quietly walked away. But who can understand the sadness of a mother? The children were still laughing happily, the kittens were still jumping, the maid was still teasing them, and Mrs. Lü was still smiling happily. The terrible thing finally happened on the first day. Ah Hua took one of the children and hid upstairs, refusing to come down no matter what, not eating or crying, so the maid had to send stinky fish and rice upstairs. My wife told me that Ah Hua had bitten the lame child to death in the kitchen!

"Ah? When did that happen?" I couldn't help but be greatly surprised.

"Probably last night." My wife's trembling voice was obviously moved. Then she said, "It's really a strange thing, there would be such a cat in the world! But do you think this is hate or love?"

I didn't answer her, I just felt that Ah Hua's behavior was too terrifying. For a long time I didn't dare to forget it, I even didn't want to see Ah Hua walk past me. I simply felt that human wisdom and emotions were not necessarily comparable to Ah Hua's level.

It was another deep night, and the humidity of the plum rain season, even if the quiet windows were tightly closed, would make you feel that the thick fog of rain would suffocate you to death. I could hardly bear my mood to write an article, and what's more, I heard Ah Hua crying woo-woo. I could hear that this cry contained a kind of love and anxiety, as if a mother had accidentally lost her son and had to call him back immediately. Sure enough, I listened carefully and quietly, and there was still little Ah Mi's voice outside the door, trembling in the fog of rain. So I quickly opened the door, hugged it in, and let it snuggle in its mother's arms, Ah Hua snuggling against its wet fur. After a while, I rushed them back to the kitchen, little Ah Mi hobbling and jumping behind its mother. It turned out that this one that hadn't died had been trampled and injured by Mrs. Lü. But I hope this injury will be better soon. The next day I didn't forget to tell the maid, "Be careful again, don't let Ah Hua bite it to death again."

After that, summer quickly passed, and little Ah Mi grew up, but there was still the original wound on its leg, and it would inevitably be disabled for life, but who would take the affairs of animals to heart?

Occasionally I asked my wife, and she said that Ah Hua had been much kinder recently, and I secretly rejoiced that little Ah Mi was very lucky; although it was disabled, wasn't it more important to be able to stay in the world? At the same time, I also thought this: if I were a veterinarian, I would use splints to tie up and correct its leg, give it more fish and meat to eat, and make it stronger, and maybe it would get better, too.

In the hot weather, people all hid in their houses, not daring to go out, only Ah Hua, but I saw it sunbathing in the courtyard several times. At first I was surprised, but later I found it was thin, and I knew it was sick. The day before yesterday, everyone smelled a stench in the courtyard, and Ah Er looked around and found Ah Hua's decaying corpse in the corner near the fish tank, it had died quietly! Who would have expected it?

The Reason Why Humans are Different from Animals

Sailing 199

— Ren Jun

Steering the helm with all my strength,

Rowing the oars with all my strength—

We are all toiling boatmen,

On this ship of "life".

The ship of "life" drifts in the dark night,

Drifts in the vast ocean.

Countless treacherous reefs lurk in the ocean,

Just one moment of carelessness,

You will surely fall for its tricks;

Countless violent white waves crouch in the ocean,

Just one moment of negligence,

You will surely meet the Dragon King of the sea.

But fear has vanished from the calm heart,

And panic cannot fly to the strong arms:

Steering the helm as usual,

Rowing the oars as usual—

Sailing straight ahead!

Grasped tightly in hand is the compass,

We will never lose our direction;

Even if the surroundings are still pitch black,

It will always be unable to hide the light of the lighthouse.

Steer the helm even more vigorously!

Row the oars even more forcefully!

Bound to the helm is an unyielding will,

Hidden under the oars is a firm conviction:

The ship of "life" always sails straight ahead—

Sailing straight through the dark night,

Sailing to the homeland of the sun!

Sailing straight through the vast ocean,

Sailing to the place full of blooming flowers!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Informal Discussions

After Reading Song Zheyuan's Letter to Fellow Compatriots in Hebei and Chahar 200

— Me

I was very surprised to suddenly see Song Zheyuan's letter to fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar in the newspaper the other day. Before I saw Mr. Song's letter to fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar, I was confused and did not carefully consider the difficulty of Mr. Song's situation, and whether his response to the environment was appropriate. But after seeing Mr. Song's letter to fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar, I was even more surprised and suspicious.

I don't know what Mr. Song means by publishing his letter to fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar? Is it because the fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar cannot forgive Mr. Song's current attitude and have doubts, so Mr. Song published such a letter to clarify his aspirations? Or is it that the fellow compatriots outside Hebei and Chahar are dissatisfied with Mr. Song's conduct and measures, so Mr. Song's letter to fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar is also to inform the fellow compatriots outside Hebei and Chahar, so that Mr. Song's attitude and ambitions can be known to the world and future generations? Or is it that Mr. Song, after being busy with paperwork, suddenly had a blow and unease in his conscience, and also had some apologies, so he published such a letter to explain himself? Therefore, before Mr. Song did not inform his fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar, it was fine, but once he informed them, it made his fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar, and those who were not from Hebei and Chahar, even more confused and inexplicable.

Mr. Song's position in North China is indeed difficult, which is well known and can be forgiven, because if Mr. Song assumes to have some advocacy, then before Mr. Song has any advocacy in our country, how can we blame Mr. Song for not being able to make the people of the country understand and forgive him? Therefore, because of Mr. Song's letter, I thought of a letter that Dr. Hu once wrote to Mr. Song. In his letter, he put forward five key points:

First, I hope that Mr. Song Zheyuan will thoroughly understand his own position. Second, I hope that Mr. Song Zheyuan understands that all enemies of the Republic of China are his enemies. Third, I hope that Mr. Song Zheyuan will use clear language to express his attitude to our friendly "neighboring country". Fourth, I hope that Mr. Song Zheyuan will thoroughly understand that his power is the power that stands on the national position.

The last point said that the national position is a whole, not a branch, and all acts of compromise and reconciliation, no matter how forgivable the intention, their traces are all destroying the unity of the country, and the people of the whole country will never forgive them. This letter was published in the 204th issue of Independent Review, and the publishing agency of the newspaper was in Beiping. I believe Mr. Song has already read this article. Now, Mr. Song's so-called equality and mutual benefit in foreign relations, seeking beneficial cooperation between the two sides, and never doing anything to betray the people's power and humiliate the country, judging from the current situation in North China, I don't know where this statement of yours comes from, so the more Mr. Song Zheyuan informs his fellow compatriots in Hebei and Chahar, the more doubts his fellow compatriots have.

Gold Panner 201

— Zhi Fu

The tide has receded towards the east. The Qiantang River—looks like a flat porcelain basin. The seawater on the river surface is tinged with yellow, as if someone had stirred it up. The green hills and sandy beaches on the opposite bank are shrouded in a hazy mist, looking from afar like they are covered with layers of transparent, light gauze.

Most of the boats sailed towards the south of the Yangtze River last night when the tide rose; now, only a few sharp-tailed sand-panning boats remain, scattered on the river, swiftly sailing like shooting stars in the summer night. ———

They sailed to the seawall of Wangjia Gaobao, and the time was just noon. Old Man Xiaogen's boat was the first to dock.

Old Man Xiaogen—extended a head from the stern of the cabin, with silvery white hair and bristly whiskers: fluttering in the wind. His face looked like a dried walnut, with more than ten deep wrinkles, and a high nose bridge, bulging between two bright eyes. He squinted his eyes and looked around the river:

———Xiaogen! Where are they going? Do you see Uncle Jiu's boat?

He then pointed to the boats on the waterway ahead.

———Uncle Jiu and the others are probably going to the Qilitang area. They are really enthusiastic, going to find "live cargo" (like fish and shrimp) there again!

———Xiaogen! "Live cargo" is valuable, should we go too?

———Don't go! I think we should just start digging sand here. Going there would be at least five or six li away, I'm afraid you can't handle that much distance!

Xiaogen said earnestly with a serious black face.

———Oh———the old man sighed, looking back at Xiaogen: a son with a strong body and muscles like a bull had long satisfied him. Why should he still be envious of others? Let them go find "live cargo".

Thinking like this, he grunted and climbed into the cabin to take out bamboo baskets and iron shovels for Xiaogen. Xiaogen, with his upper body bare, looked like a fat frog, ready to jump into the water.

———Xiaogen! You have to be careful! Your father is old, you must pay attention to quicksand.

———Dad, don't worry!

This is a wide river surface. It is more than thirty zhang away from the shore. Panning for sand would be too deep! There is no water with anything to pan for, not to mention "live cargo," which is scarce here. Then, the father and son need to plan.

———Xiaogen! Let's get closer!

———This is the firewood pier (a fort to prevent the dike from collapsing) of Wangjiabao! Doesn't the Dike Works Bureau have an order that "all boats, large and small, are not allowed to dock"? Dad! We are not allowed to dock here!

———Then!… You, you…

While they were discussing, from afar, on the dike, two policemen guarding the dike glared fiercely at them.

Page 18

——Hey! Young man! Come closer,—one of them, like a hedgehog, spoke first:—Damn it! I finally caught you today! You two are stealing dike firewood. Come closer! Let ten minutes be enough for you to take our blame!

Another one, with a broken, hoarse voice, spoke, and immediately took the foreign rifle from his shoulder and placed it in his right hand.

——Officer Sir! We are sand-panning boatmen, we are innocent! Please…

Old Man Xiaogen collapsed on the cabin floor, using all his strength to make his face turn red, and squeezed out some words from between his teeth to answer.

——Still trying to deny it? Go fool someone else, I won't be deceived by you!

"What can we do"?!

The boat came closer, and the child Xiaogen was finally taken away amidst the noisy struggle and Old Man Xiaogen's tears, in exchange for two kicks and a few slaps, considering his old age, he was let go.

The next day, people along the river spread the word: "Xiaogen, who pans for sand, committed some crime yesterday at Wangjia Gaobao and was arrested by the dike police and sentenced to two years of imprisonment"?!

Mistake 202

— Yan Ting

The wife waved her hand and said softly, "Go, I'm fine..."

The husband and I hurriedly left the small two-story house.

It was already autumn, and the streets seemed unusually quiet. Withered yellow plane tree leaves flew in the cold night wind.

I became very gloomy, and even now I can still hear the faint, slightly choked voice in my ears, the voice coming from the mouth of a seventeen- or eighteen-year-old woman with tuberculosis.

Three months ago, she still had a very strong body, two big, round, black eyes, and spoke in a loud voice with a slightly masculine tone. But now everything has changed, she has become thin and haggard...

In the factory, she was a beautiful flower, with about twelve or thirteen young male workers chasing after her at the same time. Now, her husband is one of them. He has an honest and handsome face, and a body as strong as a young bull, a promising young worker. He and she are from the same hometown, and they are the same age, so he has an advantage in the group of people who coveted this little flower.

One day, I didn't go to work. In the evening, he came to knock on the door of our cubicle. When I came out to open the door for him, I couldn't help but be shocked by his disheveled appearance. His face was bruised and swollen, blood was flowing from his lips, and one hand was wrapped in a handkerchief; however, he was still smiling happily, with an excited and resolute look on his face.

"I...I fought with that bunch of bastards..." he said in a low voice.

I stared at him worriedly for a moment: "Why? Because of jealousy?..."

He looked seriously around the room, as if he didn't hear what I said, and then silently continued:

"Because they all bullied her. One said, 'Aying, let's open a hotel,' and made obscene gestures; another simply thickened his skin and reached out to touch her breasts. I got angry at the time and fought with three of them."

"You fool, everyone is working well in the factory, why hurt everyone's feelings for a woman?..." I said a little displeasedly in a reproachful tone.

"You, you don't understand..." he opened his eyes wide, looking at me as if he were angry, and then silently opened the door and went out.

In the factory, whenever we went to work or got off work, we occasionally had the opportunity to meet, but mostly we just glanced at each other silently, or waved our hands, and then walked away as if nothing had happened.

However, one day he came to our house with Aying, both of them very excited, their faces flushed. As soon as he entered the door, he laughed loudly and said:

"Guess, Rongsheng, why are we here?..."

She stood shyly next to the table, smiling, which made her even more charming. It was here that I began to understand how this young man was so infatuated with her. I looked at them, and although I guessed six or seven points in my heart, I still pretended to be stupid and said in an incomprehensible tone:

"Can't guess, is there night work tonight?..."

They laughed heartily when they heard this, laughing so loudly that they couldn't catch their breath. Finally, they slowly restrained their smiles and said in a low voice:

"We are here to invite you to our wedding feast. We have been living together since yesterday..."

I was a little worried for them. They were young, and their monthly income was so small. They just lived together because of a temporary emotional impulse. If something unexpected happened, they would be in great danger; however, I didn't say it. I just silently expressed my comfort for their happy life.

After that, they lived according to their own wishes, full of excitement and happiness. However, soon Yin Ni occupied their hearts, and she coughed and stopped doing business. This sudden change was too strange for them. Her condition had new changes. She went to the Red Cross Hospital, and the doctor told them it was tuberculosis. He became depressed and desperate, and often came to me with tears in his eyes:

"You, Rongsheng, help me think of a way, she is about to despair..."

I was very sad. Although I couldn't help him much, I promised to think of a way for him. Now, we are stepping on the streets of September dusk, heading towards a journey of hope.

"You are young and emotional, and you don't take a step back to think..."

He hurriedly interrupted my words painfully, and called out in a sad tone:

"I...I did wrong..."

I looked and his eyes were red with anger.

Child 203

— Xiu Yang

——Starting with "Debt Collection"

The child died three minutes after being born. They say that is "landing pass" from the moment a person is born to the moment they die, they have to go through many "passes", so wealthy families specially made gold "pass clearance" ornaments for their children to be attached to their hats, saying that this can "turn bad luck into good fortune". But what about the "landing pass" where they die as soon as they are born? They only say that they came to "collect debts", and there is no way to save them.

I already have a six-year-old child who has already entered school. The child is very smart and lovely. In lonely times, he is often my teacher, because his questions and actions evoke my childhood memories: he is also my shadow, and he accepts my stubborn personality. I don't spoil this child like ordinary parents, maybe it can be said that I love him more than ordinary. I warn him not to learn all bad habits, instill in him the things that children should do, but not deprive him of his innocence—this is a lesson I learned from watching Shirley Temple's films. This child, who has earned countless benefits for Hollywood businessmen, now, his innocence has been almost completely deprived, he is just a money-making "machine" like other "cash cows". Although the audience welcomes her "matter-of-fact" non-child actions, this is undoubtedly a cruel punishment! Children should be allowed to act willfully, just as Mao Dun said in "Fun Children" "philanthropist" (to be continued)

Movie News

Nanjing Grand Theater Presents "The Great Ziegfeld" 208

Everyone who has seen the film The Great Ziegfeld unanimously believes that this film is a great masterpiece that has never been seen in the film industry since its inception. Only the head of Hollywood Pictures, MGM, has such courage and talent to make such a great attempt. William Powell, Myrna Loy, and Luise Rainer play the most important roles in the film, which is already a choice of the times. The greatness of the singing and dancing scenes can be called the artistic crystallization of the company's technical staff. The revolving stage and the flying stage are truly unprecedented spectacles. The costumes worn by the dancers in the film are novel in style and dazzling, and everywhere they adhere to the principle of "beauty". Ziegfeld was originally the leader of the Broadway singing and dancing world. He had a lot of good materials under his command. Eddie Cantor, a famous comedian in the film industry, and the late master of humor, Will Rogers, were his discoveries. His slogan is to "Glorify the America Girls", meaning to use the inherent physical beauty of American girls, with the beauty of pearls and jade, and the beauty of soft colors and melodious tunes, to create a new era in the singing and dancing world. Therefore, the show was watched by thousands of people as soon as it was staged. Now MGM has presented his commendable and moving deeds and all the singing and dancing creations he had painstakingly managed in his life to the audience at sea. It is now being screened at the Nanjing Grand Theater in this city. Film lovers in Shanghai should not miss this once-in-a-century opportunity.

"The Great Ziegfeld" 209

"Night Meeting" Accomplishes German Virtue 210

Writing the Cruel Phase of the Gold-Drenched Night Market with the Lightest and Most Beautiful Style

After the July 1st innovation, the Star Company's film production line has obviously progressed to the most active direction. "Night Meeting" has restored the "women's rights" and accomplished German virtue. After this film, one of the Star's Second Factory "Qingming Season" (directed by Ouyang Yuqian, starring Li Minghui and Zhao Dan, written by Yao Sinnong) and "Life and Death Together" (directed by Ying Yunwei, starring Yuan Muzhi and Chen Bo'er, written by Yang Hansheng), and the First Factory's "Eternal Smile" (directed by Wu Cun, starring Hu Die and Zhao Dan, written by Liu Naou) will also be completed one after another. Star also has the completed "Xiao Lingzi" (directed by Cheng Bugao, starring Tan Ying and Zhao Dan, written by Ouyang Yuqian), which is waiting to be released. The gray twilight color of the Chinese film industry in the past has now changed to a lively and thriving state.

"Night Meeting" was written by Yao Sufeng. The famous director Li Pingqian continued the masterpiece of "Peach and Plum Contending", using the lightest and most beautiful style to express the tragic state of the glittering and brilliant night Shanghai. The leading actors are Gu Lanjun, Gong Jianong, Huang Naishuang, Xie Jun, etc. Shi Fu made a cameo appearance. Gong Jianong played a blind man, deeply moving. Gu Lanjun's enthusiasm and loveliness, and Huang Naishuang's sorrowful and beautiful posture are all enough to touch the hearts of the audience. The newcomer Xie Jun played a beautiful and cruel teenager, and Li Pingqian personally regarded him as very satisfied. The release date of this film should also be in the near future.
